<span class="akn-akomaNtoso"><article class="akn-act" data-contains="originalVersion" data-name="act"><section class="akn-preface" id="preface"><span class="akn-p">Under the provisions of section 156 of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution of the Republic of South Africa, 1996</a>, the Bergrivier Municipality enacts as follows:—</span></section><span class="akn-body"><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_I" data-eId="chp_I"><h2>Chapter I<br>General provisions</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_I__part_1" data-eId="chp_I__part_1"><h2>Part 1 – Definitions</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Definitions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_1__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For the purpose of this by-law, any word or expressions to which a meaning has been assigned in the Water Services <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_1">Act</span>, 1996 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Act No 108 of 1996</a>), the Local Government: Municipal Systems Act, 2000 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/32">Act No 32 of 2000</a>) or the National Building Regulations made in terms of the National Building Regulations and Building Standards Act, 1977 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/103" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/103">Act No 103 of 1977</a>) shall bear the same meaning in this by-law and unless the context indicates otherwise and a word in any one gender shall be read as referring also, to the other gender, the singular includes the plural and vice versa, the English text prevails in the event of an inconsistency between the different text:—</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-accommodation_unit">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-accommodation_unit">accommodation unit</span>" in relation to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span>, means a building or section of a building occupied or used or intended for occupation or use for any purpose;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-account">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-account">account</span>" means an account rendered for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_3">municipal services</span> provided;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Act">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Act">Act</span>" means the Water Services Act, 1997 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1997/108" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1997/108">Act No 108 of 1997</a>), as amended from time to time;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-agreement">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-agreement">agreement</span>" means the contractual relationship between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_4">municipality</span> and a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_5">consumer</span>, whether written or deemed as provided for in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_6">municipality</span>’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-approved">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-approved">approved</span>" means approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_7">municipality</span> in writing;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-area_of_supply">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-area_of_supply">area of supply</span>" means any area within or partly within the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_8">municipality</span> to which a water service is provided;</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_agent"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_agent">authorised agent</span>" means—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> authorised by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span> to perform any act, function or duty in terms of, or to exercise any power under, this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span> to whom the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">municipality</span> has delegated the performance of certain rights, duties and obligations in respect of providing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">water supply services</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">person</span> appointed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">municipality</span> in a written contract as a service provider for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3">water services</span> to consumers on its behalf, to the extent authorised in such contract;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-average_consumption">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-average_consumption">average consumption</span>" means the average consumption of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_9">consumer</span> of a municipal service during a specific period, and is calculated by dividing the total measured consumption of that municipal service by that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_10" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_10">consumer</span> over the preceding three months by three;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-best_practicable_environmental_option">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-best_practicable_environmental_option">best practicable environmental option</span>" means the option that provides the most benefit or causes the least damage to the environment as a whole, at a cost acceptable to society, in the long term as well as in the short term;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-borehole">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-borehole">borehole</span>" means a hole sunk into the earth for the purpose of locating, abstracting or using subterranean water and includes a spring;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Building_Regulations">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Building_Regulations">Building Regulations</span>" means the National Building Regulations made in terms of the National Building Regulations and Building Standards, 1977 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/103" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/103">Act No 103 of 1977</a>) as amended;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-charges">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-charges">charges</span>" means the rate, charge, tariff, flat rate or subsidy <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_11" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_11">determined</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_council" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_12" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_12">municipal council</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-cleaning_eye">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-cleaning_eye">cleaning eye</span>" means any access opening to the interior of a discharge pipe or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-trap" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_13" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_13">trap</span> provided for the purposes of internal cleaning;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-communal_water_services">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-communal_water_services">communal water services</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_14" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_14">consumer</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_15" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_15">connection</span> through which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_16" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_16">water services</span> are supplied to more than one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_17" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_17">person</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-combined_installation">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-combined_installation">combined installation</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_18" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_18">water installation</span> used for fire-fighting and domestic, commercial or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_purposes" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_19" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_19">industrial purposes</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-commercial_consumer">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-commercial_consumer">commercial consumer</span>" means any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_20" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_20">consumer</span> other than <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-domestic_consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_21" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_21">domestic consumer</span> and indigent consumers, including, without limitation, business, industrial, government and institutional consumers;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-connecting_point">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-connecting_point">connecting point</span>" means the point at which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drainage_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_22" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_22">drainage installation</span> joins the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connecting_sewer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_23" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_23">connecting sewer</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-connecting_sewer">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-connecting_sewer">connecting sewer</span>" means a pipe owned by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_24" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_24">municipality</span> and installed by it for the purpose of conveying <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_25" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_25">sewage</span> from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drainage_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_26" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_26">drainage installation</span> on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_27" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_27">premises</span> to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_28" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_28">sewer</span> beyond the boundary of those <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_29" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_29">premises</span> or within a servitude area or within an area covered by a way-leave or by <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_30" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_30">agreement</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-connection">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-connection">connection</span>" means the point at which a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_31" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_31">consumer</span> gains access to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_32" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_32">water services</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-connection_pipe">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-connection_pipe">connection pipe</span>" means a pipe, the ownership of which is vested in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_33" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_33">municipality</span> and installed by it for the purpose of conveying water from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-main" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_34" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_34">main</span> to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_35" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_35">water installation</span>, and includes a "communication pipe" referred to in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_36" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_36">SANS</span> 0252 Part I;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-conservancy_tank">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-conservancy_tank">conservancy tank</span>" means a covered tank used for the reception and temporary retention of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_37" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_37">sewage</span> and which requires emptying at intervals;</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2" data-refersTo="#term-consumer"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-consumer">consumer</span>" means—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_1">occupier</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_2">premises</span> to which or on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_3">municipality</span> has agreed to provide <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_4">water services</span> or is actually providing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_5" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_5">water services</span>, or if there be no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_6" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_6">occupier</span>, then any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_7" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_7">person</span> who has entered into a current <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_8" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_8">agreement</span> with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_9" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_9">municipality</span> for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_10" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_10">water services</span> to or on such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_11" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_11">premises</span>, or, if there be no such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_12" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_12">person</span>, then the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_13" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_13">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_14" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_14">premises</span>; provided that where <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_15" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_15">water services</span> is provided through a single <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_16" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_16">connection</span> to a number of occupiers, it shall mean the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_17" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_17">occupier</span>, or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_18" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__list_2__item_a__term_18">person</span>, to whom the <span class="akn-term" services</span>" means, for purposes of this by-law, services provided by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_102" data-refersTo="#term-occupier">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-occupier">occupier</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_103" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_103">person</span> who occupies any (or part of any) land, building, structure or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_104" trustee, executor, administrator, judicial manager, liquidator or other legal representative;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__subsec_1__list_4__item_c" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_129" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_129">connection pipe</span> to serve the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_130" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_131">premises</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-shared_consumption">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-shared_consumption">shared consumption</span>" means the consumption by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_132" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_132">consumer</span> of a municipal service during a specific period, that is calculated by dividing the total metered consumption of that municipal service in the supply zone where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_133" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_133">consumer</span>’s <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_134" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_134">premises</span> are situated for the same period by the number of consumers within the supply zone, during that period;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-sewage">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-sewage">sewage</span>" means waste water, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_effluent" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_135" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_135">industrial effluent</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-standard_domestic_effluent" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_136" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_136">standard domestic effluent</span> and other liquid waste, either separately or in combination, but shall not include <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-stormwater" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_137" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_137">stormwater</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-sewage_disposal_system">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-sewage_disposal_system">sewage disposal system</span>" means the structures, pipes, valves, pumps, meters or other appurtenances used in the conveyance through the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_138" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_138">sewer</span> reticulation system and treatment at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_139" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_139">sewage</span> treatment plant under the control of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_140" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_140">municipality</span> and which may be used by it in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_141" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_141">connection</span> with the disposal of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_142" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_142">sewage</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-sewer">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-sewer">sewer</span>" means any pipe or conduit which is the property of or is vested in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_143" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_143">municipality</span> and which may be used for the conveyance of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_144" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_144">sewage</span> from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connecting_sewer" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_145" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_145">connecting sewer</span> and shall not include a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drain" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_146" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_146">drain</span> as defined;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-standpipe">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-standpipe">standpipe</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_147" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_147">connection</span> through which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_148" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_148">water supply services</span> are supplied to more than one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_149" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_149">person</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-standard_domestic_effluent">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-standard_domestic_effluent">standard domestic effluent</span>" means domestic <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-effluent" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_150" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_150">effluent</span> with prescribed strength characteristics as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_151" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_151">determined</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_152" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_152">municipality</span> in respect of chemical oxygen demand and settable solids as being appropriate to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_153" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_153">sewage</span> discharges from domestic <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_154" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_154">premises</span> within the jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_155" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_155">municipality</span>, but shall not include <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_effluent" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_156" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_156">industrial effluent</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-stormwater">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-stormwater">stormwater</span>" means water resulting from natural precipitation or accumulation and includes rainwater, subsoil water or spring water;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-terminal_water_fitting">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-terminal_water_fitting">terminal water fitting</span>" means <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_fitting" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_157" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_157">water fitting</span> at an outlet of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_158" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_158">water installation</span> that controls the discharge of water from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_159" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_159">water installation</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-trade_premises">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-trade_premises">trade premises</span>" means <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_160" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_160">premises</span> upon which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_effluent" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_161" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_161">industrial effluent</span> is produced;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-trap">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-trap">trap</span>" means a pipe fitting or portion of a sanitary appliance designed to retain water seal which serves as a barrier against the flow of foul air or gas, in position;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-unauthorised_service">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-unauthorised_service">unauthorised service</span>" means the receipt, use or consumption of any municipal service which is not in terms of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_162" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_162">agreement</span> with, or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_163" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_163">approved</span> by, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_164" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_164">municipality</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-water_fitting">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-water_fitting">water fitting</span>" means a component of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_165" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_165">water installation</span>, other than a pipe, through which water passes or in which it is stored;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation">water installation</span>" means the pipes and water fittings which are situated on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_166" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_166">premises</span> and ownership thereof vests in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_167" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_167">owner</span> thereof and used or intended to be used in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_168" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_168">connection</span> with the use of water on such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_169" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_169">premises</span>, and includes a pipe and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_fitting" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_170" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_170">water fitting</span> situated outside the boundary of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_171" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_171">premises</span>, which either connects to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection_pipe" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_172" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_172">connection pipe</span> relating to such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_173" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_173">premises</span> or is otherwise laid with the permission of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_174" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_174">municipality</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-water_services">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-water_services">water services</span>" means <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_175" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_175">water supply services</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_176" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_176">sanitation services</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-water_services_intermediaries">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-water_services_intermediaries">water services intermediaries</span>" has the same meaning as that assigned to it in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_177" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_177">Act</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services">water supply services</span>" has the same meaning assigned to it in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_178" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_178">Act</span> and includes for purposes of this by-law water for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_purposes" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_179" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_179">industrial purposes</span> and fire extinguishing services;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system">water supply system</span>" means the structures, aqueducts, pipes, valves, pumps, meters or other apparatus relating thereto of which the ownership vests in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_180" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_180">municipality</span> and which are used or intended to be used by it in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_181" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_181">connection</span> with the supply of water, and includes any part of the system;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-wet_industry">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-wet_industry">wet industry</span>" means an industry which discharges <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_effluent" id="sec_1__subsec_1__term_182" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1__term_182">industrial effluent</span>; and</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-working_day">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-working_day">working day</span>" means a day other than a Saturday, Sunday or public holiday.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_1__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any word or expression used in this by-law to which a meaning has been assigned in—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">he <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">Act</span> will bear that meaning; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the National <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Building_Regulations" id="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">Building Regulations</span> and Building Standards <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">Act</span>, 1997 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/103" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/103">Act No. 103 of 1977</a>), the Building Regulations will in respect of Chapter IV bear that meaning, unless the context indicates otherwise.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_1__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any reference in Chapter I of this by-law to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_1__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_3__term_1">water services</span> or services must be interpreted as referring to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services" id="sec_1__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_3__term_2">water supply services</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_1__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_3__term_3">sanitation services</span> depending on the services to which it is applicable.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_I__part_2" data-eId="chp_I__part_2"><h2>Part 2 – Application for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="chp_I__part_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_I__part_2__term_1">water services</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Application for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__term_1">water services</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_2__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> shall gain access to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__term_2">water services</span> from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_2__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__term_3">water supply system</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage_disposal_system" id="sec_2__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__term_4">sewage disposal system</span> or through any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_2__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__term_5">sanitation services</span> unless he or she has applied to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__term_6">municipality</span> on the prescribed form for such services for a specific purpose and to which such application has been agreed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may refuse to provide a water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_2__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2__term_2">connection</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_2__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_3__term_1">premises</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_3__term_2">consumer</span> are provided with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_3__term_3">water services</span>, it shall be deemed that an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_3__term_4">agreement</span> in terms of subsection (1) exists.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> must on application for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_4__term_2">water services</span> by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_4__term_3">consumer</span> inform that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_4__term_4">consumer</span> of the different levels of services available and the tariffs and/or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_2__subsec_4__term_5" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_4__term_5">charges</span> associated with each level of services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_5__term_1">consumer</span> must elect the available level of services to be provided to him or her or it.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_6__term_1">consumer</span> may at any time apply to alter the level of services elected in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_6__term_2">agreement</span> entered into, provided that such services are available or that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_6__term_3">municipality</span>’s water supply service allows for such alteration and that any costs and expenditure associated with altering the level of services will be payable by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_6__term_4">consumer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An application agreed to by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_7__term_1">municipality</span> shall constitute an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_7__term_2">agreement</span> between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_7__term_3">municipality</span> and the applicant, and such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_7__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_7__term_4">agreement</span> shall take effect on the date referred to or stipulated in such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_7__term_5" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_7__term_5">agreement</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_8__term_1">consumer</span> shall be liable for all the prescribed tariffs and/or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_2__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_8__term_2">charges</span> in respect of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_8__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_8__term_3">water services</span> rendered to him or her until the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_8__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_8__term_4">agreement</span> has been terminated in accordance with this by-law or until such time as any arrears have been paid.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In preparing an application form for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_1">water services</span> the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_2">municipality</span> will ensure that the document and the process of interaction with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_3">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_4">consumer</span> or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_5" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_5">person</span> making application are understood by that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_6" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_6">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_7" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_7">consumer</span> or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_8" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_8">person</span>. In the case of illiterate or similarly disadvantaged persons, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_9" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_9">municipality</span> will take reasonable steps to ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_2__subsec_9__term_10" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_9__term_10">person</span> is aware of and understands the contents of the application form.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An application form will require at least the following minimum information:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">ertification by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_agent" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1">authorised agent</span> that the applicant is aware of and understands the contents of the form;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">acceptance by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1">consumer</span> of the provisions of this by-law and acceptance of liability for the cost of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_2">water services</span> rendered until the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_3">agreement</span> is terminated or until such time as any arrears have been paid;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">name of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_1">consumer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">address or stand number of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d__term_1">premises</span> to or on which water servies are to be rendered or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-communal_water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d__term_2">communal water services</span> work where <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_d__term_3">water services</span> will be used;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">address where accounts will be sent;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">source of income of the applicant;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">name and address of the applicant’s employer, where appropriate;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">if water will be supplied, the purpose for which the water is to be used; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the agreed date on which the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_10__list_1__item_i__term_1">water services</span> will commence.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Water services rendered to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_11__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_11__term_1">consumer</span> are subject to the provisions of this by-law and the conditions contained in the relevant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_2__subsec_11__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_11__term_2">agreement</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12"><span class="akn-num">(12)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_1">municipality</span> refuses an application for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_2">water services</span>, is unable to render such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_3">water services</span> on the date requested for such provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_4">water services</span> to commence or is unable to render the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_5" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_5">water services</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_6" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_6">municipality</span> will inform the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_7" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_7">consumer</span> of such refusal and/or inability, the reasons therefor and, if applicable, when the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_8" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_8">municipality</span> will be able to provide such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_2__subsec_12__term_9" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_12__term_9">water services</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_3" data-eId="sec_3"><h3>3. Special agreements for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__term_1">water services</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> may enter into a special <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_2">agreement</span> for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_3">water services</span> with an applicant in accordance with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__term_4">municipality</span>’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_4" data-eId="sec_4"><h3>4. Change in purpose for which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__term_1">water services</span> are used</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the purpose for, or extent to which, any municipal service is changed, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_1">consumer</span> must promptly advise the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> of the change and enter into a new <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_3">agreement</span> with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__term_4">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_I__part_3" data-eId="chp_I__part_3"><h2>Part 3 – Tariffs and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="chp_I__part_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_I__part_3__term_1">charges</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_5" data-eId="sec_5"><h3>5. Prescribed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__term_1">charges</span> for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__term_2">water services</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">All tariffs and or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">charges</span> payable in respect of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">water services</span> rendered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3">municipality</span> in terms of this by-law, including but not limited to the payment of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_4">connection</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_5">charges</span>, fixed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_6">charges</span> or any additional <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_7">charges</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_8">interest</span> in respect of failure to pay such tariffs or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_9">charges</span> on the specified date will be set by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_10" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_10">municipality</span> by a resolution passed by the Council in accordance with:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">its tariff policy;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">any by-law in respect thereof; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">any regulations in terms of national or provincial legislation</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_6" data-eId="sec_6"><h3>6. Availability <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__term_1">charges</span> for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__term_2">water services</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, in addition to the tariffs or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">charges</span> prescribed for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">water services</span> actually provided, levy a monthly fixed charge, annual fixed charge or once-off fixed charge in respect of the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">water services</span> in accordance with—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">its tariff policy;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any by-law in respect thereof; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any regulations in terms of national or provincial legislation</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a fixed charge is levied in terms of subsection (1), it shall be payable by every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_2">consumer</span> in respect of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_3">water services</span> provided by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_4">municipality</span> to him, her or it, whether or not <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_5">water services</span> are used by him, her or it.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_I__part_4" data-eId="chp_I__part_4"><h2>Part 4 – Payment</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_7" data-eId="sec_7"><h3>7. Payment of deposit</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1">consumer</span> must on application for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_2">water services</span> and before such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_3">water services</span> will be provided by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_4">municipality</span>, deposit with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_5">municipality</span> a sum of money as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_6">determined</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_7">municipality</span> from time to time except in the case of a pre-payment <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-measuring_device" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_8">measuring device</span> being used by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_9">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may require a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2">consumer</span> to whom services are provided and who was not previously required to pay a deposit, for whatever reason, to pay a deposit on request, within a specified period.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_7__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__term_1">interest</span> shall be payable by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> on the amount of a deposit held by it in terms of this section.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_7__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4__term_1">agreement</span> for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_7__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4__term_2">water services</span> may contain a condition that a deposit shall be forfeited to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4__term_3">municipality</span> if it has not been claimed within twelve months of the termination of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_7__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4__term_4">agreement</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_8" data-eId="sec_8"><h3>8. Payment for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__term_1">water services</span> provided</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Water services provided by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2">consumer</span> shall be paid for by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3">consumer</span> at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed_tariff_or_charge" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_4">prescribed tariff or charge</span> set in accordance with sections 5 and 6, for the particular category of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_5">water services</span> provided.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1">consumer</span> shall be responsible for payment for all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_2">water services</span> provided to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_3">consumer</span> from the date of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_4">agreement</span> until the date of termination thereof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> may estimate the quantity of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_8__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__term_2">water services</span> provided in respect of a period or periods within the interval between successive measurements and may render an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account" id="sec_8__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__term_3">account</span> to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_8__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__term_4">consumer</span> for the services so estimated.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_I__part_5" data-eId="chp_I__part_5"><h2>Part 5 – Accounts</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_9" data-eId="sec_9"><h3>9. Accounts</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Monthly accounts will be rendered to consumers for the amount due and payable, at the address last recorded with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Failure by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> to render an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_2">account</span> does not relieve a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_3">consumer</span> of the obligation to pay any amount due and payable.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_I__part_6" data-eId="chp_I__part_6"><h2>Part 6 – Termination, limitation and discontinuation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="chp_I__part_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_I__part_6__term_1">water services</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_10" data-eId="sec_10"><h3>10. Termination of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__term_1">agreement</span> for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_10__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__term_2">water services</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_1">consumer</span> may terminate an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_2">agreement</span> for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_3">water services</span> by giving to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_4">municipality</span> notice in writing of his or her intention to do so.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, by notice in writing of not less than thirty working days, advise a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">consumer</span> of the termination of his, her or its <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">agreement</span> for the provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__term_4">water services</span> if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">he, she or it has not used the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">water services</span> during the preceding six months and has not made arrangements to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span> for the continuation of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">agreement</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">he, she or it has failed to comply with the provisions of this by-law and has failed to rectify such failure to comply on notice in terms of section 19;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">in terms of an arrangement made by it with another <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">water services</span> institution to provide <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">water services</span> to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_3">consumer</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> may, after having given reasonable notice, terminate an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_2">agreement</span> for services if a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_3">consumer</span> has vacated the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_4">premises</span> to which such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_5">agreement</span> relates.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_11" data-eId="sec_11"><h3>11. Limitation and/or discontinuation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_11__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__term_1">water services</span> provided</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">engineer</span> may restrict or discontinue <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">water services</span> provided in terms of this by-law—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">on failure to pay the prescribed tariffs or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">charges</span> on the date specified, in accordance with and after the procedure set out in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span>’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection has been applied;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">at the written request of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">consumer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">agreement</span> for the provision of services has been terminated in terms of section 10 and it has not received an application for subsequent services to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">premises</span> within a period of 90 (ninety) days of such termination.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the building on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">premises</span> to which services were provided has been demolished;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">consumer</span> has interfered with a restricted or discontinued service;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">emergency</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">consumer</span> has interfered, tampered or damaged or caused or permitted interference, tampering or damage to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2">water supply system</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_3">municipality</span> for the purposes of gaining access to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_4">water supply services</span> after notice by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_5">municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">on failure to comply with any other provisions of this by-law, after notice in terms of section 19 was given.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> shall not be liable for any damages or claims that may arise from the limitation or disconnection of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_11__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__term_2">water services</span> provided in terms of subsections (1), including damages or claims that may arise due to the limitation or disconnection of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services"
