id="sec_11__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__term_3">water services</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__term_4">municipality</span> in the bona fide belief that the provisions of subsection (1) applied.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_I__part_7" data-eId="chp_I__part_7"><h2>Part 7 – General provisions</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_12" data-eId="sec_12"><h3>12. Responsibility for compliance with this by-law</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_12__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_12__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> is responsible for ensuring compliance with this by-law in respect of all or any matters relating to any installation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_12__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2__term_1">consumer</span> is responsible for compliance with this by-law in respect of matters relating to the use of any installation.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_13" data-eId="sec_13"><h3>13. Exemption</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">engineer</span> may, in writing exempt an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">consumer</span>, any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">person</span> or category of owners, consumers, or other persons from complying with a provision of this by-law, subject to any conditions it may impose, if he or she is of the opinion that the application or operation of that provision would be unreasonable, provided that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__term_5">engineer</span> shall not grant exemption from any section of this by-law that may result in—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the wastage or excessive consumption of water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the evasion or avoidance of water restrictions;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">significant negative effects on public health, safety or the environment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the non-payment for services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the installation of pipes and fittings which are not <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">approved</span> in terms of this by-law and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">Act</span>, or any regulations made in terms of it, not being complied with.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may at any time after giving written notice of at least thirty days, withdraw any exemption given in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_14" data-eId="sec_14"><h3>14. Unauthorised use of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_14__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__term_1">water services</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> may gain access to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_2">water services</span> from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_3">water supply system</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage_disposal_system" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_4">sewage disposal system</span> or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_5">sanitation services</span> unless an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_6">agreement</span> has been entered into with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_7">municipality</span> for the rendering of those services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, irrespective of any other action it may take against such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">person</span> in terms of this by-law, by written notice order a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">person</span> who has gained access to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_4">water services</span> from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_5">water supply system</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage_disposal_system" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_6">sewage disposal system</span> or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_7">sanitation services</span> without an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_8">agreement</span> with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_9">municipality</span> for the rendering of those services,</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">to apply for such services in terms of sections 2 or 3; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">to undertake such work as may be necessary to ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">consumer</span> installation through which access was gained complies with the provisions of this by-law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of sections 18 and 19 shall apply to a notice in terms of subsection (2) above.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_15" data-eId="sec_15"><h3>15. Interference with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_15__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__term_1">water supply system</span> or any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_15__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__term_2">sanitation services</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> other than the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> shall manage, operate or maintain the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_3">water supply system</span> or any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_system" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_4">sanitation system</span> unless authorised by this by-law or an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_agent" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_5">authorised agent</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_1">person</span> other than the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_2">municipality</span> shall effect a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_3">connection</span> to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_4">water supply system</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage_disposal_system" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_5">sewage disposal system</span> or render any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_6" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_6">sanitation services</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_16" data-eId="sec_16"><h3>16. Interference with infrastructure</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_16__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> may unlawfully interfere with infrastructure through which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_16__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> provides <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_services" id="sec_16__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__term_3">municipal services</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">person</span> contravenes subsection (1), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">by written notice require such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> to seize or rectify the interference at his own expense within a specified period; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if it is of the opinion that the situation is a matter of urgency, without prior notice prevent or rectify the interference and recover the cost from such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_17" data-eId="sec_17"><h3>17. Obstruction of access to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_17__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__term_1">water supply system</span> or any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_17__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__term_2">sanitation services</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_17__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> shall prevent or restrict physical access to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_17__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__term_2">water supply system</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage_disposal_system" id="sec_17__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__term_3">sewage disposal system</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">person</span> contravenes subsection (1), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">by written notice require such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> to restore access at his or her own expense within a specified period; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if it is of the opinion that the situation is a matter of urgency, without prior notice restore access and recover the cost from such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_18" data-eId="sec_18"><h3>18. Signing of notices and documents</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A notice or document issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> in terms of this by-law and signed by a staff member of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> shall be deemed to have been duly issued and must on its mere production be accepted by a court as prima facie evidence of that fact.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_19" data-eId="sec_19"><h3>19. Service of notices</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any notice, order or other document that is served on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">person</span> in terms of this by-law must, subject to the provisions of the Criminal Procedure <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">Act</span> 1977 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/51" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/51">Act 51 of 1977</a>), be served personally, falling which it may regarded as having duly been served—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been left at a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span>’s village, place of residence, or business or employment in the Republic, with a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">person</span> apparently over the age of sixteen years;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been posted by registered or certified mail to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span>’s last known residential address or business address in the Republic and an acknowledgement of posting thereof from the postal service is obtained;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">person</span>’s address in the Republic is unknown, when it has been served on that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">person</span>’s agent or representative in the Republic in a manner provided for in subsections (a), (b) or (d); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">person</span>’s address and agent or representative in the Republic is unknown, when it has been placed in a conspicuous place on the property or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">premises</span>, if any, to which it relates.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any legal process is effectively and sufficiently served on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> when it is delivered to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_19__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2__term_2">municipal manager</span> or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2__term_3">person</span> in attendance at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_19__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2__term_4">municipal manager</span>’s office.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When any notice or other document must be authorised or served on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_2">occupier</span> of any property, or of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_3">person</span> who holds a right over, or in respect of it, it is sufficient if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_4">person</span> is described in the notice or other document as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_5">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_6">occupier</span> or holder of the right over or in respect of, the property, and shall not be necessary to name him.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where compliance with a notice is required within a specified number of working days, the period that is required shall commence on the date when the notice is served or when it has first been given in any other way contemplated in this by-law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_20" data-eId="sec_20"><h3>20. Authentication of documents</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every order, notice or other document requiring authentication by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> shall be sufficiently authenticated, if it is signed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_2">municipal manager</span>, by a duly authorised officer of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> or by the Manager of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_4">municipality</span>’s <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_agent" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_5">authorised agent</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Authority to authorise, as envisaged in subsection (1) must be conferred by a resolution of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span>, by a written <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-agreement" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2">agreement</span> or by a bylaw.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_21" data-eId="sec_21"><h3>21. Prima facie evidence</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In legal proceedings by or on behalf of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span>, a certificate reflecting an amount of money as being due and payable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span>, shall, if it is made under the hand of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_3">municipal manager</span>, or of a suitably qualified employee of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_4">municipality</span> who is authorised by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_5">municipal manager</span> or the Manager of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_6">municipality</span>’s <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-authorised_agent" id="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_21__hcontainer_1__term_7">authorised agent</span>, shall upon its mere production constitute prima facie evidence of the indebtedness.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_22" data-eId="sec_22"><h3>22. Power to serve and compliance with notices</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, by written notice, order an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_2">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_3">consumer</span> or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_4">person</span> who fails, by act or omission, to comply with the provisions of this by-law or of any condition imposed thereunder to remedy such breach within a period specified in the notice.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">person</span> fails to comply with a written notice served on him or her by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> in terms of this by-law within the specified period, it may take such action that in its opinion is necessary to ensure compliance, including—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">undertaking the work necessary itself and recovering the cost of such action or work from that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">consumer</span> or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">person</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">limiting or discontinuing the provision of services; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">instituting legal proceedings.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A notice in terms of subsection (1) will—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">give details of the provision of the by-law not complied with;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">give the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">consumer</span> or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3">person</span> a reasonable opportunity to make representations and state his or her case, in writing, to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_4">municipality</span> within a specified period, unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_5" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_5">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_6" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_6">consumer</span> or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_7" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_7">person</span> was given such an opportunity before the notice was issued;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">specify the steps that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2">consumer</span> of other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3">person</span> must take to rectify the failure to comply;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">specify the period within which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_2">consumer</span> or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_3">person</span> must take the steps specified to rectify such failure; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">indicate that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1">municipality</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">may undertake such work necessary to rectify the failure to comply if the notice is not complied with and that any costs associated with such work may be recovered from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_2">consumer</span> or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_3">person</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">may take any other action it deems necessary to ensure compliance.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_22__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_4__term_1">emergency</span> the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> may without prior notice undertake the work required by subsection (3)(e)(i) and recover the costs from such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_22__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_4__term_3">person</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The costs recoverable by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> in terms of subsections (3) and (4) is the full cost associated with that work and includes, but is not limited to, any exploratory investigation, surveys, plans, specifications, schedules of quantities, supervision, administration charge, the use of tools, the expenditure of labour involved in disturbing or rehabilitation of any part of a street or ground affected by the work and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-environmental_cost" id="sec_22__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__term_2">environmental cost</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_23" data-eId="sec_23"><h3>23. Power of entry and inspection</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may enter and inspect any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_23__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> for any purpose connected with the implementation or enforcement of this by-law, at all reasonable times, after having given reasonable written notice to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_23__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__term_3">occupier</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_23__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__term_4">premises</span> of the intention to do so.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any entry and inspection must be conducted in conformity with the requirements of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution of South Africa, 1996</a>, and any other law and, in particular, with strict regard to decency and order, respect for a person’s dignity, freedom and security, and personal privacy.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> may be accompanied by an interpreter and any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_2">person</span> reasonably required to assist the authorised official in conducting the inspection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1">person</span> representing the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> must, on request, provide his identification.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_24" data-eId="sec_24"><h3>24. Provision of information</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_2">occupier</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_3">consumer</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_4">person</span> within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-area_of_supply" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_5">area of supply</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_6">municipality</span> must provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_7">municipality</span> with accurate information requested by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_8">municipality</span> that is reasonably required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_24__hcontainer_1__term_9">municipality</span> for the implementation or enforcement of this by-law.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_25" data-eId="sec_25"><h3>25. False statements or information</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__term_1">person</span> shall make a false statement or furnish false information to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> or falsify a document issued in terms of this by-law.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_26" data-eId="sec_26"><h3>26. Indemnification from liability</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Neither employees of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> nor any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_2">person</span>, body, organisation or corporation acting on behalf of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_3">municipality</span> is liable for any damage arising from any omission or act done in good faith in the course of his duties unless the damage is caused by a wrongful and intentional act or negligence.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_27" data-eId="sec_27"><h3>27. Conflict of law</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If there is any conflict between this by-law and any other by-law of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span>, this by-law will prevail.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_28" data-eId="sec_28"><h3>28. Transitional arrangements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Installation work authorised by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> prior to the commencement date of this by-law or authorised <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-installation_work" id="sec_28__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__term_2">installation work</span> in progress on that date shall be deemed to have been authorised in terms of this by-law; and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> may, for a period of 90 (ninety) days after the commencement of this by-law, authorise <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-installation_work" id="sec_28__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__term_4">installation work</span> in accordance with the by-law that regulated that work immediately prior to the promulgation of this by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any reference in this by-law to a charge <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1">determined</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_council" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_2">municipal council</span> shall be deemed to be a reference to a charge <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_3">determined</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_council" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_4">municipal council</span> under the laws repealed by section 29, until the effective date of any applicable <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_5">charges</span> that may be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_6" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_6">determined</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_council" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_7" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_7">municipal council</span> in terms of this by-law, or by-law relating to credit control and debt collection, and any reference to a provision in the laws repealed by section 29 shall be deemed to be a reference to a corresponding provision in this by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any approval, consent or exemption granted under the laws repealed by section 29 shall, save for the provisions of subsection (3), remain valid.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_1">consumer</span> shall be required to comply with this by-law by altering a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_2">water installation</span> or part of it which was installed in conformity with any laws applicable immediately prior to the commencement of this by-law; provided that if, in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_3">engineer</span>, the installation, or part, is so defective or in a condition or position that could cause waste or undue consumption of water, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pollution" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_4">pollution</span> of the water supply or a health hazard, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_5" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_5">engineer</span> may by notice require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_6" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_6">consumer</span> to comply with the provisions of this by-law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_29" data-eId="sec_29"><h3>29. Repeal of existing municipal <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_29__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__term_1">water services</span> by-law</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of any by-law relating to water supply and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_services" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_1">sanitation services</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> are hereby repealed insofar as they relate to matters provided for in this by-law.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_30" data-eId="sec_30"><h3>30. Short title and commencement</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This by-law are called the Water Services By-law of the Bergrivier Municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may, by notice in the Provincial Gazette, determine that provisions of this by-law, listed in the notice, do not apply in certain areas within its area of jurisdiction listed in the notice from a date specified in the notice.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Until any notice contemplated in subsection (2) is issued, this by-law is binding.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_31" data-eId="sec_31"><h3>31. Appeals against decisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__term_1">municipality</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1">consumer</span> may appeal in writing against a decision of, or a notice issued by, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> in terms of this by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An appeal in terms of subsection (1) must be made in writing and lodged with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> within 14 (fourteen) days after a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">consumer</span> became aware of the decision or notice and must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">set out the reasons for the appeal; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">be accompanied by any security <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">determined</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">municipality</span> for the testing of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-measuring_device" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3">measuring device</span>, if it has been tested.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An appeal must be decided by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> within 14 (fourteen) days after an appeal was lodged and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_2">consumer</span> must be informed of the outcome in writing, as soon as possible thereafter.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> is final.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> may condone the late lodging of appeals or other procedural irregularities.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_32" data-eId="sec_32"><h3>32. Waste of water</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">consumer</span> shall permit—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the purposeless or wasteful discharge of water from terminal water fittings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">pipes or water fittings to leak;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the use of maladjusted or defective water fittings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">an overflow of water to persist or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">an inefficient use of water to persist.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_32__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> shall repair or replace any part of his water and sanitation installation which is in such a state of disrepair that it is either causing or is likely to cause an occurrence listed in subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_32__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_3__term_1">owner</span> fails to take measures as contemplated in subsection (2), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_32__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> shall, by written notice in terms of section 22, require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_32__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_3__term_3">owner</span> to comply with the provisions of subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_32__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_4__term_1">consumer</span> shall ensure that any equipment or plant connected to his or her <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_32__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_4__term_2">water installation</span> uses water in an efficient manner.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_32__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> may, by written notice, prohibit the use by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_32__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_5__term_2">consumer</span> of any equipment in a water or sanitation installation if, in its opinion, its use of water is inefficient. Such equipment shall not be returned to use until its efficiency has been restored and a written application to do so has been <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_32__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_5__term_3">approved</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_32__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_5__term_4">municipality</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_33" data-eId="sec_33"><h3>33. Unauthorised and illegal discharges</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_33__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> may discharge or cause or permit any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__term_2">sewage</span> to be discharged directly or indirectly into a storm water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drain" id="sec_33__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__term_3">drain</span>, river, stream or other watercourse, whether natural or artificial.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_2">occupier</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_3">premises</span> on which steam or any liquid other than potable water, is stored, processed or generated shall provide all facilities necessary to prevent any discharge or leakage of such liquid to any street, storm water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drain" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_4">drain</span> or watercourse, whether natural or artificial, except where, in the case of steam, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_5">municipality</span> has <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_6" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_6">approved</span> such discharge.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the hosing down or flushing by rainwater of an open area on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_1">premises</span> is in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> is likely to cause the discharge of objectionable matter into any street, storm water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drain" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_3">drain</span>, river, stream or other watercourse, whether natural or artificial, or to cause or contribute towards the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pollution" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_4">pollution</span> of any such watercourse, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_5">municipality</span> may, by notice, require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_6">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_7" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_7">premises</span> to take reasonable measures to prevent or minimise such discharge or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-pollution" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_8" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_8">pollution</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">person</span> may discharge or cause or permit the discharge of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any substance, including storm water, other than <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">sewage</span>, to be discharged into a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drainage_installation" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">drainage installation</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">of water from any swimming pool directly or indirectly over any road or into a gutter, storm water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drain" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">drain</span>, watercourse, open ground or private <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2">premises</span> other than the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_3">premises</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_4">owner</span> of such swimming pool;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">water from artificial fountains, reservoirs or swimming pools situated on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">premises</span> into a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drainage_installation" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_2">drainage installation</span>, without the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_3">municipality</span> and subject to the payment of relevant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_4">charges</span> and such conditions as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_5" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_5">municipality</span> may impose;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_1">sewage</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_effluent" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_2">industrial effluent</span> or other liquid or substance which—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i__term_1">engineer</span> may be offensive to or may cause a nuisance to the public;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">is in the form of steam or vapour or has a temperature exceeding 44° C at the point where it enters the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewer" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii__term_1">sewer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">has a pH value less than 6.0;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any substance of whatsoever nature likely to produce or release explosive, flammable, poisonous or offensive gases or vapours in any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewer" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_1">sewer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any substance having an open flashpoint of less than 93° C or which releases a poisonous vapour at a temperature below 93° C;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any material of whatsoever nature, including oil, grease, fat or detergents capable of causing obstruction to the flow in sewers or drains or interference with the proper operation of a sewerage treatment works;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">shows any visible signs of tar or associated products or distillates, bitumens or asphalts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_viii" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_viii"><span class="akn-num">(viii)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any substance in such concentration to produce an undesirable taste after chlorination or an undesirable odour or colour, or excessive foam;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ix" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ix"><span class="akn-num">(ix)</span><span class="akn-p">has either a greater PV or COD (Chemical Oxygen Demand) value, a lower pH value, or a higher caustic alkalinity or electrical conductivity than specified in Schedule A, without the prior approval and subject to the payment of relevant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-charges" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ix__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ix__term_1">charges</span> and such conditions as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ix__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ix__term_2">municipality</span> may impose;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x"><span class="akn-num">(x)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">contains any substance which in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__term_1">engineer</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">cannot be treated at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_aa__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_aa__term_1">sewage</span> treatment work to which it could be discharged; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">will negatively affect the treatment processes at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_bb__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_bb__term_1">sewage</span> treatment work to which it could be discharged or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_cc" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_cc"><span class="akn-num">(cc)</span><span class="akn-p">will negatively impact on the ability of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_cc__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_cc__term_1">sewage</span> treatment work to produce discharges that meet the waste water discharge standards set in terms of the National Water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_cc__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_cc__term_2">Act</span>, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/36" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/36">Act No 36 of 1998</a>), or</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi"><span class="akn-num">(xi)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">either alone or in combination with other substance may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">generate or constitute a toxic substance dangerous to the health of persons employed at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_aa__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_aa__term_1">sewage</span> treatment works or entering the council’s sewers or manholes in the course of their duties; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">be harmful to sewers, treatment plant or land used for the disposal of treated waste water; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc"><span class="akn-num">(cc)</span><span class="akn-p">adversely affect any of the processes whereby <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc__term_1">sewage</span> is treated or any re-use of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc__term_2">sewage</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-effluent" id="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_xi__list_1__item_cc__term_3">effluent</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_33__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__term_1">person</span> shall cause or permit the accumulation of grease, oil, fat or solid matter in any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-drainage_installation" id="sec_33__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__term_2">drainage installation</span> that will adversely affect its effective functioning.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, notwithstanding any other actions that may be taken in terms of this by-law, recover from any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_2">person</span> who discharges <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_effluent" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_3">industrial effluent</span> or any substance which is unauthorised or illegal all costs incurred, by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__term_4">municipality</span> as a result of such discharges, including costs that result from—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">injury to persons, damage to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_system" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1">sanitation system</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"
