data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a prosecution in terms of the National Water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Act" id="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1">Act</span>, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/36" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/36">Act No 36 of 1998</a>).</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_34" data-eId="sec_34"><h3>34. Illegal re-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-connection" id="sec_34__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__term_1">connection</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_34__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_34__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_34__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__hcontainer_1__term_1">consumer</span> whose access to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services" id="sec_34__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__hcontainer_1__term_2">water supply services</span> have been restricted or disconnected, who intentionally reconnects to services or who intentionally or negligently interferes with infrastructure through which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_services" id="sec_34__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_34__hcontainer_1__term_3">water supply services</span> are provided, shall be disconnected.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_35" data-eId="sec_35"><h3>35. Pipes in streets or public places</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_35__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_35__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_1">person</span> shall for the purpose of conveying water or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sewage" id="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_2">sewage</span> derived from whatever source, lay or construct a pipe or associated component on, in or under a street, public place or other land owned by or under the control of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_3">municipality</span>, except with the prior written permission of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_4">municipality</span> and subject to such conditions as it may impose.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_36" data-eId="sec_36"><h3>36. Use of water from sources other than the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_36__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__term_1">water supply system</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> shall use or permit the use of water obtained from a source other than the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_2">water supply system</span>, other than rain water tanks which are not connected to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_installation" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_3">water installation</span>, except with the prior approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_4">engineer</span>, and in accordance with such conditions as it may impose, for domestic, commercial or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_purposes" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_5">industrial purposes</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_36__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2__term_1">person</span> desiring the consent referred to in subsection (1) shall provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_36__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2__term_2">engineer</span> with evidence satisfactory to it that the water referred to in subsection (1) complies, whether as a result of treatment or otherwise, with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_36__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2__term_3">SANS</span> 241: Drinking Water, or that the use of such water does not or will not constitute a danger to health.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any consent given in terms of subsection (1) may be withdrawn if, in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">engineer</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a condition imposed in terms of subsection (1) is breached; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the water quality no longer conforms to the requirements referred to in subsection (2).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_36__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_4__term_1">engineer</span> may take samples of water obtained from a source, other than the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_supply_system" id="sec_36__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_4__term_2">water supply system</span> and cause the samples to be tested for compliance with the requirements referred to in subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-determined" id="sec_36__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_5__term_1">determined</span> charge for the taking and testing of the samples referred to in subsection (4) above shall be paid by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_36__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_5__term_2">person</span> to whom consent was granted in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If water obtained from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-borehole" id="sec_36__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_6__term_1">borehole</span> or other source of supply on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_36__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_6__term_2">premises</span> is used for a purpose which gives rise to the discharge of such water or a portion thereof into the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_36__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_6__term_3">municipality</span>’s sewerage system, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_36__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_6__term_4">municipality</span> may install a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-meter" id="sec_36__subsec_6__term_5" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_6__term_5">meter</span> in the pipe leading from such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-borehole" id="sec_36__subsec_6__term_6" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_6__term_6">borehole</span> or other source of supply to the point or points where it is so used.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_37" data-eId="sec_37"><h3>37. Use of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-on_site_sanitation_services" id="sec_37__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__term_1">on-site sanitation services</span> not connected to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_system" id="sec_37__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__term_2">sanitation system</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> shall use or permit the use of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-on_site_sanitation_services" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_2">on-site sanitation services</span> not connected to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span>’s <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sanitation_system" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_4">sanitation system</span> except with the prior approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_5">engineer</span>, and in accordance with such conditions as it may impose, for domestic, commercial or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-industrial_purposes" id="sec_37__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__term_6">industrial purposes</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_37__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__term_1">person</span> desiring the consent referred to in subsection (1) shall provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_37__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2__term_2">engineer</span> with evidence satisfactory to it that the sanitation facility is not likely to have a detrimental effect on heath or the environment.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any consent given in terms of subsection (1) may be withdrawn if, in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">engineer</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a condition imposed in terms of subsection (1) is breached; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the sanitation facility has a detrimental impact on health or the environment.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-engineer" id="sec_37__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_4__term_1">engineer</span> may undertake such investigations as he or she may deem necessary to determine if a sanitation facility has a detrimental impact on health or the environment.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_37__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_5__term_1">person</span> to whom consent was granted in terms of subsection (1) shall be liable for the costs associated with an investigation undertaken in terms of subsection (2) if the result of the investigation indicates that the sanitation facility has a detrimental impact on health or the environment.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_38" data-eId="sec_38"><h3>38. Offences and penalties</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_38__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">person</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">unlawfully and intentionally or negligently interfere with any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-water_services" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">water services</span> works of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">refuse or neglect to provide information or provide false information reasonably requested by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">refuse to give access required by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span> in terms of section 23;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">obstruct or hinder a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">municipality</span> in the exercise of his or her powers or performance of his or her functions or duties under this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">contravene or fail to comply with a provision of this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">contravene or fail to comply with a condition or prohibition imposed in terms of this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">contravene or fail to comply with any conditions imposed upon the granting of any application; consent, approval, concession, exemption or authority in terms of this by-law; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">fail to comply with the terms of a notice served upon him or her in terms of this by-law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_38__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">person</span> who contravenes any of the provision of subsection (1) shall be guilty of an offence and liable on conviction to:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a fine or imprisonment, or either such fine or such imprisonment or both such fine and such imprisonment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a continuing offence, and additional fine or an additional period of imprisonment or either such additional fine or such additional imprisonment or both such additional fine and imprisonment for each day on which such offence is continued, and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a further amount equal to any costs and expenses found by the court to have been incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span> as result of such contravention.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_39" data-eId="sec_39"><h3>39. Service levels</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_council" id="sec_39__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__term_1">municipal council</span> may, from time to time, and in accordance with national policy, but subject to principles of sustainability and affordability, by <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_notice" id="sec_39__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__term_2">public notice</span>, determine the service levels it is able to provide to consumers.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_council" id="sec_39__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__term_1">municipal council</span> may in determining service levels differentiate between types of consumers, domestic consumers, geographical areas and socio-economic areas.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" by-law:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" on which some sort of informal dwelling has been erected;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" id="chp_II" data-eId="chp_II"><h2>Chapter II<br>Water services intermediaries</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_40" data-eId="sec_40"><h3>40. Registration</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may by public notice require water services intermediaries or classes of water services intermediaries to register with the municipality in a manner specified in the public notice.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_41" data-eId="sec_41"><h3>41. Provision of water services</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Water services intermediaries must ensure that water services, including basic services as determined by the municipal council, are provided to such persons it is obliged to provide with water services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The quality, quantity and sustainability of water services provided by a water services intermediary must meet any minimum standards prescribed in terms of the Act and must at least be of the same standards as provided by the municipality to consumers.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_42" data-eId="sec_42"><h3>42. Charges for water services provided</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A water services intermediary may not charge for water services at a price which does not comply with any norms and standards prescribed under the Act and any additional norms and standards as may be set by the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A water services intermediary must provide subsidised water services, as determined by the municipal council in terms of the municipality’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection from time to time, and provided by the municipality to consumers at a price that is the same or less than the charges at which the municipality provides such services.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_III" data-eId="chp_III"><h2>Chapter III<br>Water supply services</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_1" data-eId="chp_III__part_1"><h2>Part 1 – Connection to water supply system</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_43" data-eId="sec_43"><h3>43. Provision of connection pipe</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an agreement for water supply services in respect of premises has been concluded and no connection pipe exists in respect of the premises, the owner shall make application on the prescribed form and pay the determined charge for the installation of such a pipe.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an application is made for water supply services which are of such an extent or so situated that it is necessary to extend, modify or upgrade the water supply system in order to supply water to the premises, the municipality may agree to the extension provided that the owner shall pay for the cost of the extension, as determined by the engineer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Only the engineer may install a connection pipe but the owner or consumer may connect the water installation to the connection pipe.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may commence any development on any premises unless the engineer has installed a connection pipe and meter. A connection point will be provided by the municipality within 15 working days after a successful agreement for water supply services in respect of premises has been concluded.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_44" data-eId="sec_44"><h3>44. Location of connection pipe</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A connection pipe provided and installed by the engineer shall—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">be located in a position determined by the engineer and be of a suitable size as determined by the engineer;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">terminate at—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the boundary of the land owned by or vested in the municipality, or over which it has a servitude or other right; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">at the outlet of the water meter or isolating valve if it is situated on the premises.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may at the request of any person agree, subject to such conditions as the engineer may impose, to a connection to a main other than that which is most readily available for the provision of water supply to the premises; provided that the applicant shall be responsible for any extension of the water installation to the connecting point designated by the municipality and for obtaining at his cost, any servitudes over other premises that may be necessary.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An owner must pay the determined connection charge in advance before a water connection can be effected.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_45" data-eId="sec_45"><h3>45. Provision of single water connection for supply to several consumers on the same premises</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of section 43, only one connection pipe to the water supply system may be provided for the supply of water to any premises, irrespective of the number of accommodation units, business units or consumers located on such premises.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where the owner, or the person having the charge or management of any premises on which several accommodation units are situated, requires the supply of water to such premises for the purpose of supply to the different accommodation units, the engineer may, in its discretion, provide and install either—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a single measuring device in respect of the premises as a whole or any number of such accommodation units; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a separate measuring device for each accommodation unit or any number thereof.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where the engineer has installed a single measuring device as contemplated in subsection (2) (a), the owner or the person having the charge or management of the premises, as the case may be—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">must, if the municipality so requires, install and maintain on each branch pipe extending from the connection pipe to the different accommodation units—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a separate measuring device; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">an isolating valve; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">will be liable to the municipality for the charges for all water supplied to the premises through such a single measuring device, irrespective of the different quantities consumed by the different consumers served by such measuring device.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding subsection (1), the municipality may authorise that more than one connection pipe to be provided on the water supply system for the supply of water to any premises comprising sectional title units if, in the opinion of the municipality, undue hardship or inconvenience would be caused to any consumer on such premises by the provision of only one connection pipe.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the provision of more than one connection pipe is authorised by the municipality under subsection (4), the tariffs and charges for the provision of a connection pipe is payable in respect of each water connection so provided.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_46" data-eId="sec_46"><h3>46. Interconnection between premises or water installations</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_46__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_46__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An owner of premises shall ensure that no interconnection exists between—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the water installation on his or her premises and the water installation on other premises; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">where several accommodation units are situated on the same premises, the water installations of the accommodation units;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p">unless he or she has obtained the prior written consent of the municipality, and complies with any conditions that it may have imposed.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_47" data-eId="sec_47"><h3>47. Disconnection of water installation from the connection pipe</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The engineer may disconnect a water installation from the connection pipe and remove the connection pipe if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the agreement for supply has been terminated in terms of section 10 and it has not received an application for a subsequent supply of water to the premises served by the pipe within a period of 90 days of such termination, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the building on the premises concerned has been demolished, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_47__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">on termination of an agreement for the provision of water supply services in accordance with the municipality’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_2" data-eId="chp_III__part_2"><h2>Part 2 – Communal water services works</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_48" data-eId="sec_48"><h3>48. Provision of a water services work for water supply to several consumers</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may install a communal standpipe for the provision of water supply services to several consumers at a location it considers appropriate, provided that a majority of consumers, who in the opinion of the engineer, constitute a substantial majority, and to whom water services will be provided by the standpipe, has been consulted by him or the municipality and informed of the level of service, tariffs that will be payable and location of the work.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may provide communal water supply services through a communal installation designed to provide a controlled volume of water to several consumers.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_3" data-eId="chp_III__part_3"><h2>Part 3 – Temporary water supply services</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_49" data-eId="sec_49"><h3>49. Water supplied from a hydrant</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_49__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may authorise a temporary supply of water to be taken from one or more fire hydrants specified by it, subject to such conditions and for any period that may be prescribed by him and payment of such applicable charges, including a deposit, as may be determined by the municipal council from time to time.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_49__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person who wishes to obtain a temporary supply of water referred to in subsection (1) must apply for such a water supply service in terms of section 2 and must pay a deposit determined by the municipal council from time to time.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_49__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The supply of water in terms of subsection (1) must be measured and the applicant shall provide a portable water meter and all other fittings and apparatus necessary, to the satisfaction of the engineer, for the temporary supply of water from a hydrant.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_4" data-eId="chp_III__part_4"><h2>Part 4 – Standards and general conditions of supply</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_50" data-eId="sec_50"><h3>50. Quantity, quality and pressure</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Water supply services provided by the municipality must comply with the minimum standards set for the provision of water supply services in terms of section 9 of the Act.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_51" data-eId="sec_51"><h3>51. Testing of pressure in water supply systems</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_51__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_51__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may, on application by an owner and on payment of the determined charge, determine and furnish the owner with the amount of the pressure in the water supply system relating to his premises over such period as the owner may request.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_52" data-eId="sec_52"><h3>52. Specific conditions of supply</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Notwithstanding the undertaking in section 50, the granting of a supply of water by the municipality shall not constitute an undertaking by it to maintain at any time or any point in its water supply system—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an uninterrupted supply, subject to the provisions of regulations 4 and 14 of Regulation 22355 promulgated in terms of the Act on 8 June 2003; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a specific pressure or rate of flow in such supply other than requires in terms of regulation 15(2) of Regulation 22355 promulgated in terms of the Act on 8 June 2003.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may, subject to the provisions of subsection (1)(b), specify the maximum pressure to which water will be supplied from the water supply system.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_52__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If an owner of consumer requires—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">that any of the standards referred to in subsection (1); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a higher standard of service than specified in section 50;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p">be maintained on his premises, he or she shall take the necessary steps to ensure that the proposed water installation is able to meet such standards.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may, in an emergency, interrupt the supply of water to any premises without prior notice.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If in the opinion of the engineer the consumption of water by a consumer adversely affects the supply of water to another consumer, he may apply such restrictions as he may consider fit, to the supply of water to consumer in order to ensure a reasonable supply of water to the other consumer and must inform that consumer about the restrictions.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality shall not be liable for any damage to property caused by water flowing from any water installation that is left open when the water supply is re-instated, after an interruption in supply.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every steam boiler, hospital, industry and any premises which requires, for the purpose of the work undertaken on the premises, a continuous supply of water shall have a storage tank, which must comply with the specification for water storage tanks as stipulated in SANS 0252 Part 1, with a capacity of not less than 24 hours water supply calculated as the quantity required to provide the average daily consumption, where water can be stored when the continuous supply is disrupted.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No consumer shall resell water supplied to him by the municipality except with the written permission of the municipality, which may stipulate the maximum price at which the water may be resold, and may impose such other conditions as the municipality may deem fit.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_5" data-eId="chp_III__part_5"><h2>Part 5 – Measurement of water supply services</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_53" data-eId="sec_53"><h3>53. Measuring of quantity of water supplied</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer must provide a measuring device designed to provide either a controlled volume of water, or an uncontrolled volume of water, to a consumer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality must, at regular intervals, measure the quantity of water supplied through a measuring device designed to provide an uncontrolled volume of water.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any measuring device and its associated apparatus through which water is supplied to a consumer by the municipality, shall be provided and installed by the engineer, shall remain its property and may be changed and maintained by the engineer when he consider it necessary to do so.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may install a measuring device, and its associated apparatus, at any point on the service pipe.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the engineer installs a measuring device on a service pipe in terms of subsection (4), he may install a section of pipe and associated fittings between the end of its connection pipe and the meter, and that section shall form part of the water installation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the engineer installs a measuring device together with its associated apparatus on a service pipe in terms of subsection (4), the owner shall—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">provide a place satisfactory to the engineer in which to install it;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that unrestricted access is available to it at all times;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">be responsible for its protection and be liable for the costs arising from damage to it, excluding damage arising from normal fair wear and tear;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that no connection is made to the pipe in which the measuring device is installed between the measuring device and the connection pipe serving the installation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">make provision for the drainage of water which may be discharged from the pipe, in which the measuring device is installed, in the course of work done by the engineer on the measuring device; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_6__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">not use, or permit to be used on any water installation, any fitting, machine or appliance which causes damage or which, in the opinion of the engineer, is likely to cause damage to any meter.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person other than the engineer shall:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">disconnect a measuring device and its associated apparatus from the pipe on which they are installed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">break a seal which the engineer has placed on a meter; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_7__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">in any other way interfere with a measuring device and its associated apparatus.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the engineer considers that, a measuring device is a meter whose size is unsuitable because of the quantity of water supplied to premises, he may install a meter of a size that he considers necessary, and may recover the determined charge for the installation of the meter from the owner of the premises.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may require the installation, at the owner’s expense, of a measuring device to each dwelling unit, in separate occupancy, on any premises, for use in ascertaining the quantity of water supplied to each such unit; but where controlled volume water-delivery systems are used, a single measuring device may otherwise be used for more than one unit.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_54" data-eId="sec_54"><h3>54. Quantity of water supplied to consumer</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">For the purposes of ascertaining the quantity of water that has been measured by a measuring device that has been installed by the engineer and that has been supplied to a consumer over a specific period, it will, for the purposes of this by-law, be presumed except in any criminal proceedings, unless the contrary is proved, that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the quantity, where the measuring device designed to provide an uncontrolled volume of water, is the difference between measurements taken at the beginning and end of that period;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the quantity, where the measuring device designed to provide a controlled volume of water, is the volume dispensed by the measuring device;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the measuring device was accurate during that period; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the entries in the records of the municipality were correctly made; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">if water is supplied to, or taken by, a consumer without having passed through a measuring device, the estimate by the municipality of the quantity of that water shall be presumed, except in any criminal proceedings, to be correct unless the contrary is proved.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where water supplied by the municipality to any premises is in any way taken by the consumer without the water passing through any measuring device provided by the municipality, the municipality may, for the purpose of rendering an account, estimate, in accordance with subsection (3), the quantity of water supplied to the consumer during the period that water is so taken by the consumer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_54__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">For the purposes of subsection (2), an estimate of the quantity of water supplied to a consumer shall, as the municipality may decide, be based either on—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the average monthly consumption of water on the premises recorded over three succeeding measuring periods after the date on which an irregularity referred to in subsection (2) has been discovered and rectified, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the average monthly consumption of water on the premises during any three consecutive measuring periods during the twelve months immediately before the date on which an irregularity referred to in subsection (2) was discovered.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Nothing in this by-law shall be construed as imposing on the municipality an obligation to cause any measuring device installed by the engineer on any premises to be measured at the end of every month or any other fixed period, and the municipality may estimate the quantity of water supplied over any period during the interval between successive measurements of the measuring device and render an account to a consumer for the quantity of water so estimated.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Until the time when a measuring device has been installed in respect of water supplied to a consumer, the estimated or shared consumption of that consumer during a specific period, must be based on the average consumption of water supplied to the specific supply zone within which the consumer’s premises are situated, during a specific period.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where in the opinion of the engineer it is not reasonably possible or cost effective to measure water that is supplied to each consumer within a determined supply zone, the municipality may in terms of its tariff policy determine a basic tariff or charge to be paid by each consumer within that zone irrespective of actual consumption.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality must within seven days, on receipt of a written notice from the consumer and subject to payment of the determined charge, measure the quantity of water supplied to the consumer at a time, or on a day, other than that upon which it would normally be measured.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a contravention of section 53 (7) occurs, the consumer must pay to the municipality the cost of whatever quantity of water was, in the opinion by the municipality, supplied to him.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_55" data-eId="sec_55"><h3>55. Defective measurement</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_55__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_55__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a consumer has reason to believe that a measuring device, used for measuring water, which was supplied to him or her by the municipality is defective he or she may take the steps as provided for in the municipality’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_56" data-eId="sec_56"><h3>56. Special measurement</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_56__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the engineer requires, for purposes other than charging for water consumed, to ascertain the quantity of water which is used in a part of a water installation, may, by written notice, advise the owner concerned of his intention to install a measuring device at any point in the water installation that he may specify.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_56__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The installation of a measuring device referred to in subsection (1), its removal, and the restoration of the water installation after such a removal shall be carried out at the expense of the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_56__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of sections 53 (6) and 53 (7) shall apply, insofar as they may be applicable, in respect of a measuring device that has been installed in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_57" data-eId="sec_57"><h3>57. No reduction of amount payable for water wasted</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_57__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_57__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A consumer shall not be entitled to a reduction of the amount payable for water wasted or lost in a water installation.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_6" data-eId="chp_III__part_6"><h2>Part 6 – Audit</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_58" data-eId="sec_58"><h3>58. Water audit</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_58__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may require a consumer, within one month after the end of a financial year of the municipality, to undertake a water audit at his own cost.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_58__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The audit must at least involve and report—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the amount of water used during the financial year;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the amount paid for water for the financial year;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of people living on the stand or premises;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of people permanently working on the stand or premises;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the seasonal variation in demand through monthly consumption figures;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the water pollution monitoring methods;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">the current initiatives for the management of the demand for water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">the plans to manage their demand for water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a comparison of the report with any report that may have been made during the previous three years;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">estimates of consumption by various components of use; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">a comparison of the above factors with those reported in each of the previous three years, where available.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_7" data-eId="chp_III__part_7"><h2>Part 7 – Installation work</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_59" data-eId="sec_59"><h3>59. Approval of installation work</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an owner wishes to have installation work done, he or she must first obtain the municipality’s written approval; provided that approval shall not be required in the case of water installations in dwelling units or installations where no fire installation is required in terms of SANS 0400, or in terms of any Municipal by-law, or for the repair or replacement of an existing pipe or water fitting other than a fixed water heater and its associated protective devices.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Application for the approval referred to in subsection (1) shall be made on the prescribed form and shall be accompanied by—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the determined charge, if applicable; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">copies of the drawings as may be determined by the municipality, giving information in the form required by Clause 4.1.1 of SANS Code 0252: Part I;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a certificate certifying that the installation has been designed in accordance with SANS Code 0252: Part I by a professional engineer.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of subsections (1) and (2) shall not apply to a qualified plumber who replaces a fixed water heater or its associated protective devices.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Authority given in terms of subsection (1) shall lapse at the expiry of a period of twenty-four months.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A complete set of approved drawings of installation work must be available at the site of the work at all times until the work has been completed, where approval was required in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If installation work has been done in contravention of subsection (1) or (2), the municipality may by written notice require the owner of the premises concerned to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">rectify the contravention within a specified period;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if work is in progress, to cease the work; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_6__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to remove all such work which does not comply with this by-law.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_60" data-eId="sec_60"><h3>60. Provision and maintenance of water installations</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An owner must provide and maintain his water installation at his own cost and except where permitted in terms of subsection (2), must ensure that the installation is situated within the boundary of his premises.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Before doing work in connection with the maintenance of a portion of his water installation, which is situated outside the boundary of his premises, an owner shall obtain the written consent of the municipality or the owner of the land on which the portion is situated, as the case may be.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_61" data-eId="sec_61"><h3>61. Persons permitted to do installation and other work</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Only a plumber, a person working under the control of a plumber, or another person authorised in writing by the municipality, shall be permitted to:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">do installation work other than the replacement or repair of an existing pipe or water fitting;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">replace a fixed water heater or its associated protective devices;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">inspect, disinfect and test a water installation, fire installation or storage tank;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">service, repair or replace a back flow preventer; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">install, maintain or replace a meter provided by an owner in a water installation.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall require or engage a person who is not a plumber to do the work referred to in subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_61__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_61__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection (1) the municipality may permit a person who is not a plumber to do installation work on his own behalf on premises owned and occupied solely by himself and his immediate household, provided that such work must be inspected and approved by a plumber at the direction of the engineer.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_62" data-eId="sec_62"><h3>62. Technical requirements for a water installation</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_62__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_62__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the requirement that a certificate be issued in terms of section 59, all water installations shall comply with SANS 0252 Part 1 and all fixed electrical storage water heaters shall comply with SANS 0254.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_63" data-eId="sec_63"><h3>63. Use of pipes and water fittings to be authorised</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall, without the prior written authority of the engineer, install or use a pipe or water fitting in a water installation within the municipality’s area of jurisdiction unless it is included in the Schedule of Approved Pipes and Fittings as compiled by the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Application for the inclusion of a pipe or water fitting in the Schedule referred to in subsection (1) must be made on the form prescribed by the municipality and be accompanied by the prescribed charge.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A pipe or water fitting may be not be included in the Schedule referred to in subsection (1) unless it—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">bears the standardisation mark of the South African Bureau of Standards in respect of the relevant SANS specification issued by the Bureau; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">bears a certification mark issued by the SANS to certify that the pipe or water fitting complies with an SANS Mark specification or a provisional specification issued by the SANS, provided that no certification marks shall be issued for a period exceeding two years; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">is acceptable to the municipality.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, in respect of any pipe or water fitting included in the Schedule, impose such additional conditions, as it may consider necessary in respect of the use or method of installation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_63__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A pipe or water fitting shall be removed from the Schedule if it—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">no longer complies with the criteria upon which its inclusion was based; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is no longer suitable for the purpose for which its use was accepted.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The current Schedule shall be available for inspection at the office of the municipality at any time during working hours.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may sell copies of the current Schedule at a determined charge.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_64" data-eId="sec_64"><h3>64. Labelling of terminal water fittings and appliances</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_64__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_64__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_64__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_64__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">All terminal water fittings and appliances using or discharging water shall be marked, or have included within the packaging of the item, the following information:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_64__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the range of pressure in kPa over which the water fitting or appliance is designed to operate.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_64__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the flow rate, in litres per minute, related to the design pressure range, provided that this information shall be given for at least the following water pressures: 20 kPa, 100kPa and 400 kPa.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_65" data-eId="sec_65"><h3>65. Water demand management</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_65__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In any water installation where the dynamic water pressure is more than 200 kPa at a shower control valve, and where the plumbing has been designed to balance the water pressures on the hot and cold water supplies to the shower control valve, a shower head with a maximum flow rate of greater than 10 litres per minute must not be installed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_65__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The maximum flow rate from any tap installed on a wash hand basin must not exceed 6 litres per minute.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_8" data-eId="chp_III__part_8"><h2>Part 8 – Water pollution, restriction and wasteful use of water</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_66" data-eId="sec_66"><h3>66. Owner to prevent pollution of water</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_66__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_66__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_66__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_66__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An owner shall provide and maintain approved measures to prevent the entry of a substance, which may be a danger to health or adversely affect the potability of water or affect its fitness for use, into—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_66__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the water supply system; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_66__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any part of the water installation on his or her premises.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_67" data-eId="sec_67"><h3>67. Water restrictions</h3>
