<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may by public notice to prevent the wasteful use of water in terms of section 32 or in the event of a water shortage, drought or flood—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">prohibit or restrict the consumption of water in the whole or part of its area of jurisdiction in general or for—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">specified purposes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">during specified hours of the day or on specified days; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">in a specified manner; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">determine and impose—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">limits on the quantity of water that may be consumed over a specified period;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">charges additional to those prescribed in respect of the supply of water in excess of a limit contemplated in subsection (1)(b)(i); and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a general surcharge on the prescribed charges in respect of the supply of water; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">impose restrictions or prohibitions on the use or manner of use or disposition of an appliance by means of which water is used or consumed, or on the connection of such appliances to the water installation.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may limit the application of the provisions of a notice contemplated by subsection (1) to specified areas and categories of consumers, premises and activities, and may permit deviations and exemptions from, and the relaxation of, any of the provisions on reasonable grounds.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">take, or by written notice require a consumer at his or her own expense to take, such measures, including the installation of measurement devices and devices for restricting the flow of water, as may in its opinion be necessary to ensure compliance with a notice published in terms of subsection (1); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">discontinue or, for such period as it may deem fit, limit the supply of water to any premises in the event of a contravention on such premises or failure to comply with the terms of a notice published in terms of subsection (1), subject to notice in terms of section 22; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">shall where the supply has been discontinued, restore it only when the determined charge for discontinuation and reconnecting the supply has been paid.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of this section shall also apply in respect of water supplied directly by the municipality to consumers outside its area of jurisdiction, notwithstanding anything to the contrary in the conditions governing such supply, unless otherwise specified in the notice published in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_9" data-eId="chp_III__part_9"><h2>Part 9 – Fire services connections</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_68" data-eId="sec_68"><h3>68. Connection to be approved by the municipality</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_68__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer shall be entitled in his absolute discretion to grant or refuse an application for the connection of a fire extinguishing installation to the municipality’s main.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_68__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No water shall be supplied to any fire extinguishing installation until a certificate that the municipality’s approval in terms of section 59 has been obtained and that the installation complies with the requirements of these and any other by-law of the municipality, has been submitted.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_68__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If in the engineer’s opinion a fire extinguishing installation, which he has allowed to be connected to the municipality’s main, is not being kept in proper working order, or is otherwise not being properly maintained, or is being used for purpose other than fire fighting, that shall be entitled either to require the installation to be disconnected from the main or itself to carry out the work of disconnecting it at the consumer’s expense.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_69" data-eId="sec_69"><h3>69. Special provisions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_69__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_69__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of SANS 0252-1 shall apply to the supply of water for fire fighting purposes.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_70" data-eId="sec_70"><h3>70. Dual and combined installations</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_70__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_70__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">All new buildings erected after the commencement of this by-law, must comply with the following requirements in relation to the provision of fire extinguishing services:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">If boosting of the system is required, a dual pipe system must be used, one for fire extinguishing purposes and the other for general domestic purposes.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Combined installations shall only be permitted where no booster pumping connection is provided on the water installation. In such cases a fire hydrant must be provided by the municipality, at the consumer’s expense, within 90 metres of the property to provide a source of water for the fire tender to use in extinguishing the fire.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Combined installations where a booster pumping connection is provided, shall only be permitted when designed and certified by a professional engineer.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_70__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">All pipes and fittings must be capable of handling pressures in excess of 1 800 kPa, if that pressure could be expected when boosting takes place and must be capable of maintaining their integrity when exposed to fire conditions.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_71" data-eId="sec_71"><h3>71. Connection pipes for fire extinguishing services</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">After the commencement of this by-law, a single connection pipe for both fire (excluding sprinkler systems) and potable water supply services shall be provided by the engineer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer shall provide and install, at the cost of the owner a combination meter on the connection pipe referred to in (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A separate connection pipe shall be laid and used for every fire sprinkler extinguishing system unless the engineer gives his approval to the contrary.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A connection pipe must be equipped with a measuring device that will not obstruct the flow of water while the device is operating.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_72" data-eId="sec_72"><h3>72. Valves and meters in connection pipes</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_72__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_72__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every connection pipe to a fire extinguishing installation must be fitted with valves and a measuring device which shall be:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">supplied by the engineer at the expense of the consumer;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">installed between the consumer’s property and the main; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_72__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">installed in such position as may be determined by the engineer.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_73" data-eId="sec_73"><h3>73. Meters in fire extinguishing connection pipes</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_73__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_73__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer shall be entitled to install a water meter in any connection pipe used solely for fire extinguishing purposes and the owner of the premises shall be liable for all costs in so doing if it appears to the municipality that water has been drawn from the pipe for purposes other than for the purpose of extinguishing a fire.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_74" data-eId="sec_74"><h3>74. Sprinkler extinguishing installation</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sprinkler installation may be installed directly to the main, but the municipality may not be deemed to guarantee any specified pressure at any time.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_75" data-eId="sec_75"><h3>75. Header tank or double supply from main .</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The consumer must install a header tank at such elevation as will compensate for any failure or reduction of pressure in the municipality’s main for its sprinkler installation, unless this installation is provided with a duplicate supply from a separate main.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The main pipe leading from a header tank to the sprinkler installation may be in direct communication with the main, provided that the main pipe must be equipped with a reflux valve which, if for any reason the pressure in the main fails or is reduced, will shut off the supply from the main.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a sprinkler installation is provided with a duplicate supply from a separate main, each supply pipe must be equipped with a reflux valve situated within the premises.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_76" data-eId="sec_76"><h3>76. Sealing of private fire hydrants .</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_76__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except where a system is a combined system with a combination meter, all private hydrants and hose-reels must be sealed by the municipality and the seals must not, except for the purposes of opening the hydrant or using the hose when there is a fire, be broken by any person other than by the municipality in the course of servicing and testing.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_76__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The consumer must give the municipality at least 48 hours notice prior to a fire extinguishing installation being serviced and tested.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_76__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The cost of resealing hydrants and hose-reels shall be borne by the consumer except when the seals are broken by the municipality’s officers for testing purposes.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_76__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_76__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any water consumed through a fire installation or sprinkler system shall be paid for by the consumer at the charges determined by the municipality.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_III__part_10" data-eId="chp_III__part_10"><h2>Part 10 – General provisions</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_77" data-eId="sec_77"><h3>77. Notification of boreholes</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may sink a borehole on premises situated in a dolomite area, and before sinking a borehole a person must determine if the premises on which the borehole is to be sunk are situated within a dolomite area.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may, by public notice, require—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the owner of any premises within any area of the municipality upon which a borehole exists or, if the owner is not in occupation of such premises, the occupier to notify it of the existence of a borehole on such premises, and provide it with such information about the borehole that it may require; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the owner or occupier of any premises who intends to sink a borehole on the premises, to notify it on the prescribed form of its intention to do so before any work in connection sinking it is commenced.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may require the owner or occupier of any premises who intends to sink a borehole, to undertake an environmental impact assessment of the intended borehole, to the satisfaction of the municipality, before sinking it.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Boreholes are subject to any requirements of the National Water Act, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/36" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/36">Act No 36 of 1998</a>).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may by notice to an owner or occupier or by public notice, require an owner or occupier who has an existing borehole that is used for water supply services to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">obtain approval from it for the use of a borehole for potable water supply services in accordance with sections 6, 7 and 22 of the Act; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">adhere to conditions imposed by it in respect of the use of a borehole for water services; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to pay a fixed charge imposed by it in respect of the use of such a borehole.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_78" data-eId="sec_78"><h3>78. Sampling of water</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may take samples of water obtained from a source, authorised in terms of section 6 or 7 of the Act, other than the water supply system for domestic purposes and cause the samples to be tested for compliance with any national standards prescribed in terms of section 9 of the Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_78__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_78__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The prescribed charge for the taking and testing of the samples referred to in subsection (1) shall be paid by the person to whom approval to use the water for potable water was granted in terms of section 6(1) of the Act.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_79" data-eId="sec_79"><h3>79. Supply of non-potable water by municipality</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may on application in terms of section 3 agree to supply non-potable water to a consumer, subject to such terms and conditions as the municipality may impose.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any supply of water agreed to in terms of subsection (1) shall not be used for domestic or any other purposes, which, in the opinion of the municipality, may give rise to a health risk.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No warranty, expressed or implied, shall apply to the purity of any non-potable water supplied by the municipality or its suitability for the purpose for which the supply was granted.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The supply of non-potable water shall, both as to condition and use, be entirely at the risk of the consumer, who shall be liable for any consequential damage or loss arising to himself, herself or others arising directly or indirectly there from, including the consequences of any bona fide fault of the municipality or the malfunction of a treatment plant.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_80" data-eId="sec_80"><h3>80. Testing of pressure in water supply systems</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_80__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_80__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, on application by an owner and on payment of the prescribed charge, determine and furnish the owner with the value of the pressure in the water supply system relating to his or her premises over such period as the owner may request.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_81" data-eId="sec_81"><h3>81. Pipes in streets or public places</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_81__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_81__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall for the purpose of conveying water derived from whatever source, lay or construct a pipe or associated component on, in or under a street, public place or other land owned by, vested in, or under the control of any municipality, except with the prior written permission of that municipality and subject to such conditions as it may impose.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_82" data-eId="sec_82"><h3>82. Use of grey water</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_82__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_82__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall use grey water or permit such water to be used, except with the prior written permission of the municipality and subject to such conditions as it may impose.</span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_IV" data-eId="chp_IV"><h2>Chapter IV<br>Sanitation services</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_1" data-eId="chp_IV__part_1"><h2>Part 1 – Standards and general provisions</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_83" data-eId="sec_83"><h3>83. Standards for sanitation services</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_83__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_83__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Sanitation services provided by the municipality will comply with the minimum standards set for the provision of sanitation services in terms of the section 9 of the Act.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_84" data-eId="sec_84"><h3>84. Objectionable discharge to sewage disposal system</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person shall discharge, or permit the discharge or entry into the sewage disposal system of any sewage or other substance—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">which does not comply with the standards and criteria prescribed in sections 109 to 112 below;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">which contains any substance in such concentration as will produce or be likely to produce in the effluent produces for discharge at any sewage treatment plant or sea outfalls discharge point or in any public water any offensive, or otherwise undesirable taste, colour, odour, temperature or any foam;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">which may prejudice the re-use of treated sewage or adversely affect any of the processes whereby sewage is purified for re-use, or treated to produce sludge for disposal;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">which contains any substance or thing of whatsoever nature which is not amenable to treatment to a satisfactory degree at a sewage treatment plant or which causes or is likely to cause a breakdown or inhibition of the processes in use at such plant;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">which contains any substance or thing of whatsoever nature which is of such strength, or which is amenable to treatment only to a degree as will result in effluent from the sewage treatment plant or discharge from any sea outfalls not complying with standards prescribed under the National Water Act, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/36" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/36">Act No. 36 of 1998</a>);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">which may cause danger to the health or safety of any person or may be injurious to the structure or materials of the sewage disposal system or may prejudice the use of any ground used by the municipality for the sewage disposal system, other than in compliance with the permissions issued in terms of this by-law; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">which may inhibit the unrestricted conveyance of sewage through the sewage disposal system.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall cause or permit any storm water to enter the sewage disposal system.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, by written notice, order the owner or occupier to conduct, at his or her cost, periodic expert inspections of the premises in order to identify precautionary measures which would ensure compliance with this by-law and to report such findings to an authorised agent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_84__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_84__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If any person contravenes any provision of subsection (1) or subsection (2) he or she shall within twelve hours, or earlier if possible, advise the municipality of the details of the contravention and the reasons for it.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_2" data-eId="chp_IV__part_2"><h2>Part 2 – On-site sanitation services and associated services</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_85" data-eId="sec_85"><h3>85. Application for infrastructure</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_85__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If and agreement for on site sanitation and associated services in accordance with section 2 exists and no infrastructure in connection therewith exists on the premises, the owner must immediately make application on the approved form and—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">pay the prescribed charge for the installation of necessary infrastructure; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">with the approval by the municipality and at the request of the owner, install the connecting sewer or on site sanitation services in accordance with the specifications of the municipality.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_85__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_85__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A municipality may specify the type of on site sanitation services to be installed.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_86" data-eId="sec_86"><h3>86. Services associated with on-site sanitation services</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_86__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The removal or collection of conservancy tank contents, night soil or the emptying of pits will be undertaken by the municipality in accordance with a removal and collection schedule determined by the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_86__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_86__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Copies of the collection and removal schedule will be available on request.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_87" data-eId="sec_87"><h3>87. Charges in respect of services associated with on-site sanitation services</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_87__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_87__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Charges in respect of the removal or collection of conservancy tank contents, night soil or the emptying of pits will cover all the operating and maintenance costs in the removal of the pit contents, transportation to a disposal site, the treatment of the contents to achieve a sanitary condition and the final disposal of any solid residues shall be payable in terms of the municipality’s tariff policy when the service is rendered.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_88" data-eId="sec_88"><h3>88. Installation of on-site sanitation services</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_88__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_88__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an agreement for on-site sanitation services in respect of premises has been concluded, or if it is not reasonably possible or cost effective for the municipality to install a connecting sewer, the owner must install sanitation services specified by the municipality, on the site unless the service is a subsidised service that has been determined by the municipality in accordance with the municipality’s Credit Control and Debt Collection By-law.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_89" data-eId="sec_89"><h3>89. Ventilated improved pit latrines</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, on such conditions as it may prescribe, having regard to the nature and permeability of the soil, the depth of the water table, the size of, and access to, the site and the availability of a piped water supply, approve the disposal of human excrement by means of a ventilated improved pit (VIP) latrine.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A ventilated improved pit latrine must have—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a pit of 2m³ capacity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">lining as required;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a slab designed to support the superimposed loading; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">protection preventing children from falling into the pit;</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A ventilated improved pit latrine must conform to the following specifications:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the pit must be ventilated by means of a pipe, sealed at the upper end with durable insect proof screening fixed firmly in place;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the ventilation pipe must project not less than 0.5m above the nearest roof, must be of at least 150mm in diameter, and must be installed vertically with no bend;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the interior of the closet must be finished smooth so that it can be kept in a clean and hygienic condition. The superstructure must be well-ventilated in order to allow the free flow of air into the pit to be vented through the pipe;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the opening through the slab must be of adequate size as to prevent fouling. The rim must be raised so that liquids used for washing the floor do not flow into the pit. It shall be equipped with a lid to prevent the egress of flies and other insects when the toilet is not in use;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">must be sited in a position that is independent of the dwelling unit;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">must be sited in positions that are accessible to road vehicles having a width of 3.0m in order to facilitate the emptying of the pit;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">in situations where there is the danger of polluting an aquifer due to the permeability of the soil, the pit must be lined with an impermeable material that is durable and will not crack under stress;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">in situations where the ground in which the pit is to be excavated is unstable, suitable support is to be given to prevent the collapse of the soil; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the latrine must have access to water for washing hands.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_90" data-eId="sec_90"><h3>90. Septic tanks and treatment plants</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, on such conditions as it may prescribe, approve the disposal of sewage or other effluent by means of septic tanks or other on-site sewage treatment plants.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A septic tank or other sewage treatment plant on a site must not be situated closer than 3 metres to any dwelling unit or to any boundary of the premises on which it is situated.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Effluent from a septic tank or other on-site sewage treatment plant must be disposed of to the satisfaction of the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A septic tank must be watertight, securely covered and provided with gas-tight means of access to its interior adequate to permit the inspection of the inlet and outlet pipes and adequate for the purpose of removing sludge.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A septic tank serving a dwelling unit must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">have a capacity below the level of the invert of the outlet pipe of not less than 500 litres per bedroom, subject to a minimum capacity below such an invert level of 2 500 litres;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">have an internal width of not less than 1 metre measured at right angles to the direction of the flow;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">have an internal depth between the cover and the bottom of the tank of not less than 1,7metre; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_5__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">retain liquid to a depth of not less than 1,4metre.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Septic tanks serving premises other than a dwelling unit must be designed and certified by a professional civil engineer registered as a member of the engineering Council of South Africa.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No rain water, storm-water, or effluent other than that approved by the municipality may be discharged into a septic tank.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_91" data-eId="sec_91"><h3>91. French drains</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, on such conditions as it may prescribe having regard to the quantity and the nature of the effluent and the nature of the soil as determined by the permeability test prescribed by the South African Bureau of Standards, approve the disposal of waste-water or other effluent by means of french drains, soakage pits or other approved works.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A french drain, soakage pit or other similar work shall not be situated closer than 5m to any dwelling unit or to any boundary of any premises on which it is situated, nor in any such position that will, in the opinion of the municipality, cause contamination of any borehole or other source of water which is, or may be, used for drinking purposes, or cause dampness in any building.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The dimensions of any french drain, soakage pit or other similar work shall be determined in relation to the absorbent qualities of the soil and the nature and quantity of the effluent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">French drains serving premises other than a dwelling house must be designed and certified by a professional Civil engineer registered as a member of the engineering Council of South Africa.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_92" data-eId="sec_92"><h3>92. Conservancy tanks</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, on such conditions as it may prescribe; approve the construction of a conservancy tank and ancillary appliances for retention of sewage or effluent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No rain water, storm-water, or effluent other than approved by the municipality may be discharged into a conservancy tank.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No conservancy tank must be used as such unless—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the invert of the tank slopes towards the outlet at a gradient of not less than 1 in 10;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the tank is gas and water tight;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the tank has an outlet pipe, 100mm in internal diameter, made of wrought iron, cast iron or other approved material, and except if otherwise approved by the municipality, terminating at an approved valve and fittings for connection to the municipality’s removal vehicles;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the valve and fittings referred to in paragraph (c) or the outlet end of the pipe, as the case may be, are located in a chamber that has hinged cover approved by the engineer and which is situated in a position required by the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">access to the conservancy tank must be provided by means of an approved manhole fitted with a removable cast iron cover placed immediately above the visible spigot of the inlet pipe.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, having regard to the position of a conservancy tank or of the point of connection for a removal vehicle, require the owner or consumer to indemnify the municipality, in writing, against any liability for any damages that may result from rendering of that service as a condition for emptying the tank.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the municipality’s removal vehicle has to traverse private premises for the emptying of a conservancy tank, the owner shall provide a roadway at least 3.5m wide, so hardened as to be capable of withstanding a wheel load of 4 metric tons in all weather, and shall ensure that no gateway through which the vehicle is required to pass to reach the tank, shall be less than 3.5m wide for such purposes.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner or occupier of premises on which a conservancy tank is installed shall at all times maintain the tank in good order and condition to the satisfaction of the municipality.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_93" data-eId="sec_93"><h3>93. Operation and maintenance of on-site sanitation services</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_93__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_93__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The operation and maintenance of on-site sanitation services and all costs pertaining to it remains the responsibility of the owner of the premises, unless the on-site sanitation services are subsidised services determined in accordance with the municipality’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_94" data-eId="sec_94"><h3>94. Disused conservancy and septic tanks</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_94__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_94__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an existing conservancy tank or septic tank is no longer required for the storage or treatment of sewage, or if permission for its use is withdrawn, the owner must either cause it to be completely removed or to be completely filled with earth or other suitable material, provided that the engineer may require a tank to be dealt with in another way, or approve its use for other purposes, subject to any conditions specified by him.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_3" data-eId="chp_IV__part_3"><h2>Part 3 – Sewage disposal</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_95" data-eId="sec_95"><h3>95. Obligation to connect to sanitation system</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All premises on which sewage is produced must be connected to the municipality’s sanitation system if a connecting sewer is available or if it is reasonably possible or cost effective for the municipality to install a connecting sewer, unless approval for the use of on-site sanitation services was obtained in accordance with section 37.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, by notice, require the owner of premises not connected to the municipality’s sanitation system to connect to the sanitation system.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An owner of premises, who is required to connect those premises to the municipality’s sanitation system in accordance with subsection (1), must inform the municipality in writing of any sanitation services, provided by the municipality on the site, which will no longer required as a result of the connection to the sanitation system.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner will be liable for any charge payable in respect of sanitation services on the site, until an agreement for rendering those services has been terminated in accordance with the municipality’s by-law relating to credit control and debt collection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the owner fails to connect premises to the sanitation system after having had a notice in terms of subsection (2) the municipality, notwithstanding any other action that it may take in terms of this by-law, may impose a penalty determined by it.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_96" data-eId="sec_96"><h3>96. Provision of connecting sewer</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_96__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If an agreement for sanitation services in respect of premises has been concluded in accordance with section 2 and no connecting sewer exists in respect of the premises, the owner shall make application on the prescribed form, and—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">pay the tariffs and charges determined by the municipality for the installation of a connecting sewer.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">with the approval by the municipality and at the request of the owner, install the connecting sewer in accordance with any specifications of the municipality.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_96__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an application is made for sanitation services which are of such an extent or so situated that it will become necessary to extend, modify or upgrade the sanitation system in order to provide sanitation services to any premises, the municipality may agree to the extension only if the owner pays or undertakes to pay for the cost, as determined by the engineer, of the extension, modification or upgrading of the services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_96__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Only the engineer may install or approve an installed connecting sewer; but the owner or consumer may connect the sanitation installation to the connection pipe.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_96__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may commence any development on any premises unless the engineer has installed a connecting sewer.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_97" data-eId="sec_97"><h3>97. Location of connecting sewer</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A connecting sewer that has been provided and installed by the engineer or owner in terms of section 96 must-</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">be located in a position determined by the engineer and be of a suitable size determined by the engineer; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">terminate at</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the boundary of the premises; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">at the connecting point if it is situated on the premises</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In reaching with an owner concerning the location of a connecting sewer, the municipality shall ensure that the owner is aware of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">practical restrictions that may exist regarding the location of a connecting sewer pipe;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the cost implications of the various possible locations of the connecting sewer;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">whether or not the municipality requires the owner to fix the location of the connecting sewer by providing a portion of his or her water installation at or outside the boundary of his or her premises, or such agreed position inside or outside his or her premises where the connection is required, for the municipality to connect to such installation.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The engineer may at the request of the owner of premises, approve, subject to any conditions that he may impose, a connection to a connecting sewer other than one that is most readily available for the provision of sanitation services to the premises; in which event the owner shall be responsible for any extension of the drainage installation to the connecting point designated by the municipality and for obtaining, at his own cost, any servitude over other premises that may be necessary.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where an owner is required to provide a sewage lift as provided for in terms of the Building Regulations, or the premises are at a level where the drainage installation cannot discharge into the sewer by gravitation, the rate and time of discharge into the sewer has to be subject to the approval of the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner of premises must pay the connection charges and tariffs determined by the municipality before a connection to the connecting sewer can be effected.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_98" data-eId="sec_98"><h3>98. Provision of one connecting sewer for several consumers on same premises</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of section 97, only one connecting sewer to the sanitation system may be provided for the disposal of sewage from any premises, irrespective of the number of accommodation units of consumers located on such premises.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_98__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where the owner, or the person having the charge or management of any premises on which several accommodation units are situated, requires the disposal of sewage from such premises for the purpose of disposal from the different accommodation units, the municipality may, in its discretion, provide and install either—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a single connecting sewer in respect of the premises as a whole or any number of such accommodation units; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a separate connecting sewer for each accommodation unit or any number thereof.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where the municipality has installed a single connecting sewer as contemplated in subsection (2) (a), the owner or the person having the charge or management of the premises, as the case may be—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">must if the municipality so requires, install and maintain on each branch pipe extending from the connecting sewer to the different accommodation units—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a separate connecting sewer; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">an isolating valve;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">will be liable to the municipality for the tariffs and charges for all sewage disposed from the premises through such a single connecting sewer, irrespective of the different quantities disposed by the different consumers served by such connecting sewer.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding subsection (1), the municipality may authorise that more than one connecting sewer be provided in the sanitation system for the disposal of sewage from any premises comprising sectional title units or if, in the opinion of the municipality, undue hardship or inconvenience would be caused to any consumer on such premises by the provision of only one connecting sewer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the provision of more than one connecting sewer is authorised by the municipality under subsection (4), the tariffs and charges for the provision of a connecting sewer are payable in respect of each sewage connection so provided.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_99" data-eId="sec_99"><h3>99. Interconnection between premises</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_99__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_99__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An owner of premises must ensure, unless he has obtained the prior approval of the municipality and complies with any conditions that it may have imposed, that no interconnection exists between the drainage installation on his premises and the drainage installation on any other premises.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_100" data-eId="sec_100"><h3>100. Disconnection of draining installation from connecting sewer</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_100__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_100__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_100__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_100__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may disconnect a drainage installation from the connecting sewer and remove the connecting sewer if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_100__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the agreement for provision has been terminated in terms of section 11 and it has not received an application for subsequent provision to the premises served by the sewer within a period of 90 days of such termination; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_100__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the building on the premises concerned has been demolished.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_4" data-eId="chp_IV__part_4"><h2>Part 4 – Sewage delivered by road haulage</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_101" data-eId="sec_101"><h3>101. Acceptance of sewage delivered by road haulage</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_101__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_101__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A municipality may, at its discretion, and subject to such conditions as it may specify, accept sewage for disposal delivered to the municipality’s sewage treatment plants by road haulage.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_102" data-eId="sec_102"><h3>102. Written permission for delivery of sewage by road haulage</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_102__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall discharge sewage into the municipality’s sewage treatment plants by road haulage except with the written permission of the municipality and subject to such period and any conditions that may be imposed terms of the written permission.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_102__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The charges for any sewage delivered for disposal to the municipality’s sewage treatment plants shall be assessed by the municipality in accordance with the prescribed tariffs or charges.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_103" data-eId="sec_103"><h3>103. Conditions for delivery of sewage by road haulage</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_103__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_103__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When sewage is delivered by road haulage—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_103__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the time of delivery shall be arranged in consultation with the municipality; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_103__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the nature and composition of the sewage shall be established to the satisfaction of the municipality prior to the discharge thereof and no person shall deliver sewage that does not comply with the standards laid down in terms of this by-law.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_104" data-eId="sec_104"><h3>104. Withdrawal of permission for delivery of sewage by road haulage</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_104__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may withdraw any permission, after giving written notice if its intention to a person permitted to discharge sewage by road haul if the person—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">fails to ensure that the sewage so delivered conforms to the standards prescribed in Schedule "A" or in the written permission; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">fails or refuses to comply with any notice lawfully served on him or her in terms of this by-law or contravenes any provisions of this by-law or any condition imposed on him or her in terms of any permission granted to him or her; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">fails to pay the assessed charges in respect of any sewage delivered.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_5" data-eId="chp_IV__part_5"><h2>Part 5 – Purified sewage</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_105" data-eId="sec_105"><h3>105. Use of purified sewage</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_105__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may on application in terms of section 2, agree to supply purified sewage to a consumer, subject to such terms and conditions as the municipality may impose.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_105__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No warranty, expressed or implied, shall be supplied by the municipality in respect of the suitability of the purified sewage for the purpose for which the supply was granted.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_105__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The supply of purified sewage shall, both as to condition and use, be entirely at the risk of the consumer, who shall be liable for any consequential damage or loss arising to himself, herself or others arising directly or indirectly there from, including the consequences of any bona fide fault of the municipality or the malfunction of a treatment plant.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_6" data-eId="chp_IV__part_6"><h2>Part 6 – Disposal of industrial effluent and trade premises</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_106" data-eId="sec_106"><h3>106. Application for disposal of industrial effluent</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person must apply for approval to discharge industrial effluent into the sewage disposal system of the municipality in terms of section 2(1) and on the prescribed form attached as Schedule B to this by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may, if in its opinion the capacity of a sewage disposal system is sufficient to permit the conveyance and effective treatment and lawful disposal of the industrial effluent, for such period and subject to such conditions it may impose, grant written permission to discharge industrial effluent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of Chapter I will mutatis mutandis apply to any permission to discharge industrial effluent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who wishes to construct or cause to be constructed, a building which shall be used as a trade premises, shall at the time of lodging a building plan in terms of section 4 of the National Building Regulations and Building Standards Act, 1977 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/103" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/103">Act No. 103 of 1977</a>), also lodge applications for the provision of sanitation services and for permission to discharge industrial effluent in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_107" data-eId="sec_107"><h3>107. Unauthorised discharge of industrial effluent</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_107__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_107__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall discharge or cause or permit to be discharged into the sewage disposal system any industrial effluent except with and in terms of the written permission of the municipality and in accordance the provisions of this part.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_107__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_107__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person to whom such permission is granted shall pay to the municipality any prescribed charges.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_108" data-eId="sec_108"><h3>108. Quality standards for disposal of industrial effluent</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_108__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person to whom permission has been granted must ensure that no industrial effluent is discharged into the sewage disposal system of the municipality unless it complies with the standards and criteria set out in Schedule A hereto.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_108__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may by writing in the permission concerned, relax or vary the standards in Schedule A, provided that the municipality is satisfied that any such relaxation or variation represents the best practicable environmental option.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_108__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In determining whether relaxing or varying the standards in Schedule A represents the best practicable environmental option a municipality will consider—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">whether the applicant’s undertaking is operated and maintained at optimal levels;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">whether technology used by the applicant represents the best available option to the applicant’s industry and, if not, whether the installation of such technology would entail unreasonable cost to the applicant;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">whether the applicant is implementing a programme of waste minimisation which complies with national and local waste minimisation standards to the satisfaction of the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the cost to the municipality of granting the relaxation or variation; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the environmental impact or potential impact of such a relaxation or variation.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_108__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Test samples may be taken at any time by a duly qualified sampler to ascertain whether the industrial effluent complies with Schedule A or any other standard laid down in a written permission.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_109" data-eId="sec_109"><h3>109. Conditions for disposal of industrial effluent</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_109__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may in the written permission or at any time, by written notice, require a person to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">subject the industrial effluent to such preliminary treatment as in the opinion of the municipality will ensure that the industrial effluent conforms to the standards prescribed in Schedule A before being discharged into the sewage disposal
