system;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">install such equalising tanks, valves, pumps, appliances, meters and other equipment as in the opinion of the municipality will be necessary to control the rate and time of discharge into the sewage disposal system in accordance with the conditions imposed by it;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">install for the conveyance of his or her industrial effluent into the sewage disposal system at a given point, a drainage installation separate from the drainage installation for waste water and standard domestic effluent and may prohibit such person from disposing of his or her industrial effluent at any other point and from disposing of his or her waste water and standard domestic effluent by means other than into a sewage disposal system;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">construct on any pipe conveying his or her industrial effluent to any sewer, a service access hole or stop-valve in such position and of such dimensions and materials as the municipality may prescribe;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">provide all such information as may be required by the municipality to enable it to assess the tariffs or charges due to the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">provide adequate facilities such as level or overflow detection devices, standby equipment, overflow catch-pits, or other appropriate means to prevent a discharge into the sewage disposal system which is in contravention of this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">cause any meter, gauge or other device installed in terms of this Section to be calibrated by an independent authority at the cost of that person at such intervals as required by the municipality and copies of the calibration to be forwarded to it; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">cause his or her industrial effluent to be analysed as often and in such manner as may be prescribed by the municipality and provide it with the results of these tests when completed.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_109__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The cost of any treatment, plant, works or analysis which the person mentioned in subsection (1) may be required to carry out, construct or install in terms of subsection (1) shall be borne by the said person.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_109__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The written permission of the municipality must be obtained for any proposed changes to the composition of industrial effluent discharged into the sewage disposal system.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_109__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event that industrial effluent that does not comply with the standards in Schedule A or the written permission issued in respect of that process or premises, is discharged into the sewage disposal system, the municipality must be informed of the incident and the reasons therefor within twelve hours of such discharge.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_110" data-eId="sec_110"><h3>110. Withdrawal of written permission for disposal of industrial effluent</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_110__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may withdraw any permission, after giving written notice if its intention to a person permitted to discharge industrial effluent into the sewage disposal system if the person—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">fails to ensure that the industrial effluent discharged conforms to the industrial effluent standards prescribed in Schedule A of this by-law or the written permission;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">fails or refuses to comply with any notice lawfully served on him or her in terms of this by-law or contravenes any provisions of this by-law or any condition imposed in terms of any permission granted to him or her; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">fails to pay the assessed charges in respect of any industrial effluent discharged.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_110__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_110__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may on withdrawal of any written permission—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in addition to any steps prescribed in this by-law, and on written notice authorise the closing or sealing of the connecting sewer of the said premises to any sewer for such charge as may be prescribed in the municipality’s tariff of charges; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">refuse to accept any industrial effluent until it is satisfied that adequate steps have been taken to ensure that the industrial effluent to be discharged conforms with the standards prescribed in this by-law.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_111" data-eId="sec_111"><h3>111. Sea outfalls</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of this part shall apply equally to industrial effluent discharged into any of the municipality or its authorised agent’s sea outfalls, subject to any additional conditions specific to sea outfalls that may be imposed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where industrial effluent is accepted for discharge into a sea outfall it shall be delivered to the point of acceptance approved by the municipality or its authorised agent by means of a pipeline constructed and maintained by the permitted person at his or her expense.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No industrial effluent shall be accepted for discharge into a sea outfall unless—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">it complies with the standards and criteria set out in Schedule A; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">it is proved to the satisfaction of the municipality or its authorised agent, that such effluent—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">is not toxic to marine fauna or flora;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">contains no constituents in concentrations which can create a nuisance on the beaches or in the sea, or a health hazard or which may have an adverse effect on bathing or other recreational areas;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">contains no floating material;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">contains no substance which may be prejudicial or injurious to the municipality or its authorised agent’s sea outfalls and associated sumps, sewers, plant and equipment or to its employees;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">contains no materials capable of creating a nuisance by frothing;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">contain no standard domestic effluent; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">it complies with any applicable standards in terms of the National Water Act, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/36" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/36">Act No. 36 of 1998</a>).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality or its authorised agent may relax or vary the standards and criteria in Schedule A, provided that such relaxation or variation shall not constitute a relaxation or variation of those matters referred to in subsection (3).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The delivery pipeline from the premises concerned to the point of acceptance shall be maintained in a proper condition and free from all leaks.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Acceptance of the industrial effluent shall be subject to review at any time.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_7" data-eId="chp_IV__part_7"><h2>Part 7 – Measurement of quantity of effluent discharged to sewage disposal system</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_112" data-eId="sec_112"><h3>112. Measurement of quantity of standard domestic effluent discharged</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_112__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The quantity of standard domestic effluent discharged shall be determined by a percentage of water supplied by the municipality; provided that where the municipality is of the opinion that such a percentage in respect of specific premises is excessive, having regard to the purposes for which water is consumed on those premises, the municipality may reduce the percentage applicable to those premises to a figure which, in its opinion and in the light of the available information, reflects the proportion between the likely quantity of sewage discharged from the premises and the quantity of water supplied thereto.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_112__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a premises is supplied with water from a source other than or in addition to the municipality’s water supply system, including abstraction from a river or borehole, the quantity of standard domestic effluent will be a percentage of the total water used on that premises as may be reasonably estimated by the municipality.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_113" data-eId="sec_113"><h3>113. Measurement of quantity of industrial effluent discharged</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The quantity of industrial effluent discharged into the sewage disposal system shall be determined—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">where a measuring device is installed by the quantity of industrial effluent discharged from a premises as measured through that measuring device; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">until such time as a measuring device is installed by a percentage of the water supplied by the municipality to that premises, according to Part II in Schedule B.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may require the owner of any premises to incorporate in any drainage installation conveying industrial effluent to a sewer, any control meter or gauge or other device of an approved type and in the control of the municipality for the purpose of ascertaining to the satisfaction of the municipality, the tempo, volume and composition of the effluent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may install and maintain any meter, gauge or device referred to in subsection (2) at the expense of the owner of the premises on which it is installed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where premises are supplied with water from a source other than or in addition to the municipality’s water supply system, including abstraction from a river or borehole, the quantity of standard industrial effluent will be a percentage of the total water used on that premises as may be reasonably estimated by the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a portion of the water supplied to the premises forms part of the end product of any manufacturing process or is lost by reaction or evaporation during the manufacturing process or for any other reason, the municipality may on application reduce the assessed quantity of industrial effluent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may at its discretion enter into an agreement with any person discharging industrial effluent into the sanitation system, establishing an alternative method of assessing the quantity and tempo of effluent so discharged.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Charges relating to the quality of industrial effluent will be based on the formula for industrial effluent discharges as prescribed in Schedule C.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following conditions apply in respect of the assessment of the quality of industrial effluent discharged:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">each customer must conduct the prescribed tests, on a regular schedule as provided for in the approval to discharge industrial effluent, and report the results to the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the municipality may conduct random compliance tests to correlate with those used in subsection (a) and, if discrepancies are found, the values of the municipality shall, except for the purpose of criminal proceedings, be presumed to be correct and further tests may be required by the municipality to determine, at the cost of the customer, the values for the formula;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">The average of the values of the different analysis results of 24 hourly composite or snap samples of the effluent, taken during the period of charge, will be used to determine the quality charges payable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">in the absence of a complete daily set of 24 hourly composite or snap samples, the average of not less than two values of the sampled effluent, taken during the period of charge, will be used to determine the charges payable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">in order to determine the strength (Chemical oxygen demand, suspended solids concentration, ammonia concentration, and orthophosphate concentration) in the effluent as well as the concentration of the metals, pH value and conductivity, the municipality will use the tests normally used by municipalities for these respective purposes. Details of the appropriate test may be ascertained from the municipality or the SANS. Test results from a laboratory, accredited by the municipality, will have precedence over those of the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the formula is calculated on the basis of the different analysis results of individual snap or composite samples and the period of treatment for calculation shall not be less than one full 24-hour period; unless evidence, is submitted to the municipality that a lesser period is actually applicable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">the terms of the disincentive formula cannot assume a negative value;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">the total system values for quality charges shall remain constant for an initial period of one month, but in any case not longer than twelve months from the date of commencement of theses charges, after the expiry of which time they may be amended or revised from time to time depending on such changes in the analysis results or further samples, as may be determined from time to time: provided that the municipality in its discretion in any particular case, may levy the minimum charges prescribed in section 5 without taking any samples;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">whenever the municipality takes a sample, one half of it must be made available to the customer;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">for the purpose of calculating the quantity of effluent discharged from each point of discharges of effluent, the total quantity of water consumed on the premises shall be allocated to the several points of discharge as accurately as is reasonably practicable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">the costs of conveying and treating industrial effluent shall be determined by the municipality and shall apply with effect from a date determined by the municipality; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_l" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_8__list_1__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">in the discretion of the municipality, the charges for industrial effluent may be charged to a fixed monthly charge determined by taking into consideration the effluent strengths, the volume and the economic viability of micro and small industries.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_114" data-eId="sec_114"><h3>114. Reduction in the quantity determined in terms of sections 112 and 113</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_114__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person shall be entitled to a reduction in the quantity determined in terms of sections 112 and 113 in the event that the quantity of water on which the percentage is calculated was measured during a period were water was wasted or a leakage was undetected if the consumer demonstrates to the satisfaction of the municipality that the said water was not discharged into the sewage disposal system.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_114__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The reduction in the quantity shall be based on the quantity of water loss through leakage or wastage during the leak period.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_114__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The leak period shall be either the measuring period immediately prior to the date of repair of the leak or the measurement period during which the leak is repaired, whichever results in the greater reduction in the quantity.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_114__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The quantity of water loss shall be calculated as the consumption for the leak period less an average consumption, based on the preceding 3 (three) months, for the same length of time. In the event of no previous consumption history being available the average water consumption will be determined by the municipality, after due consideration of all relevant information.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_114__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">There shall be no reduction in the quantity if the loss of water directly or indirectly resulted from the consumer’s failure to comply with or is in contravention of these or other by-law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_115" data-eId="sec_115"><h3>115. Charges in respect of "on-site" sanitation services</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_115__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_115__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Charges in respect of the removal or collection of conservancy tank contents, night soil or the emptying of pits will cover all the operating and maintenance costs arising from the removal of the pit contents, its transportation to a disposal site, the treatment of the contents to achieve a sanitary condition and the final disposal of any solid residues and are payable by the owner.</span><span class="akn-p">The additional charge for industrial effluent for the disposal of high strength sewage to a waste water treatment plant shall be determined in accordance with the formula for the calculation of effluent discharge charges as included in Schedule C.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_8" data-eId="chp_IV__part_8"><h2>Part 8 – Drainage installations</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_116" data-eId="sec_116"><h3>116. Construction or installation of drainage installations</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_116__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_116__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An owner must provide and maintain his drainage installation at his own expense, unless the installation constitutes a basic sanitation facility as determined by the municipality, and except where otherwise approved by the municipality, must ensure that the installation is situated within the boundary of his premises.</span></span></span><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_116__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may prescribe the point in the sewer, and the depth below the ground, at which any drainage installation is to be connected and the route to be followed by the drain to the connecting point and may require the owner not to commence the construction or connection of the drainage installation until the municipality’s connecting sewer has been laid.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_116__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An drainage installation that has been constructed or installed must comply with any applicable specifications in terms of the Building Regulations and any standard prescribed in terms of the Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_116__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall permit the entry of any liquid or solid substance whatsoever, other than clean water for testing purposes, to enter any drainage installation before the drainage installation has been connected to the sewer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_116__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where premises are situated in the 1 in 50 years flood plain, the top level of all service access holes, inspection chambers and gullies must be above the 1 in 50 years flood level.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_116__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">After the completion of any drainage installation, or after any alteration to any drainage installation is completed, the plumber responsible for the execution of the work must submit to the building inspection section of the municipality a certificate certifying that the work was completed to the standards set out in the building regulations, this by-law and any other relevant law or by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_116__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No rainwater or storm-water, and no effluent other than an effluent that has been approved by the municipality, may be discharged into a drainage installation.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_117" data-eId="sec_117"><h3>117. Drains</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_117__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_117__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Drains passing through ground which in the opinion of the engineer is liable to movement, shall be laid on a continuous bed of river sand or similar granular material not less than 100mm thick under the barrel of the pipe and with a surround of similar material and thickness, and the joints of such drains must be flexible joints approved by the engineer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_117__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_117__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A drain or part of it may only be laid within, or either passes under or through a building, with the approval of the engineer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_117__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_117__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A drain or part of it which it is laid in an inaccessible position under a building may not bend or be laid at a gradient.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_117__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_117__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a drain passes through or under a wall, foundation or other structure, adequate precautions shall be taken to prevent the discharge of any substance to the drain.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_118" data-eId="sec_118"><h3>118. Drains in streets or public places</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_118__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_118__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall for the purpose of conveying sewage derived from whatever source, lay or construct a drain on, in or under a street, public place or other land owned by, vested in, or under the control of the municipality, except with the prior written permission of the municipality and subject to such conditions as it may impose.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_119" data-eId="sec_119"><h3>119. Construction by municipality</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_119__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_119__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipality may agree with the owner of any premises that any drainage work which such owner desires, or is required to construct in terms of this by-law or the Building Regulations, will be constructed by the municipality against payment, in advance or on demand, of all costs associated with such construction.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_120" data-eId="sec_120"><h3>120. Maintenance of drainage installation</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_120__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner or occupier of any premises must maintain any drainage installation and any sewer connection on such premises at his own cost.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_120__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who requests the municipality to clear a drainage installation will be liable to pay the prescribed tariff.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_120__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A municipality may, on the written application of the owner or occupier of any premises, inspect and test the drainage installation of such premises or any section thereof and recover from the owner or occupier the cost of such inspection and test, calculated at the rate specified in the prescribed tariff or charges.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_120__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where any part of a drainage installation is used by two or more owners or occupiers, they shall be jointly and separately liable for the maintenance of the installation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_120__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner of any premises must ensure that all manholes and cleaning eyes on the premises are permanently visible and accessible.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_121" data-eId="sec_121"><h3>121. Installation of pre-treatment facility</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_121__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_121__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A municipality may require that any new premises must be provided with a minimum pre-treatment facility of a type specified by it prior to that premises being connected to the sewage disposal system.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_122" data-eId="sec_122"><h3>122. Protection from ingress of floodwaters</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_122__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_122__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a premises is situated in the 1 in 50 years flood plain the top level of service access holes, inspection chambers and gullies is to be above the 1 in 50 years flood level, except, in the case of service access holes and inspection chambers, where the cover is secured in place by approved means.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_123" data-eId="sec_123"><h3>123. Disconnection of drainage installations</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_123__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_123__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except for the purpose of carrying out maintenance or repair work, no drainage installation may be disconnected from the connection point.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_123__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_123__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where any part of a drainage installation is disconnected from the remainder because it will no longer be used, the disconnected part must be destroyed or entirely removed from the premises on which it was used, unless the municipality approves otherwise.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_123__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_123__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When a disconnection has been made after all the requirements of the Building Regulations in regard to disconnection have been complied with, the engineer must upon the request of the owner, issue a certificate certifying that the disconnection has been completed in terms of the Building Regulations and that any charges raised in respect of the disconnected portion of the drainage installation shall cease to be levied from the end of the month preceding the first day of the month following the issue of such certificate.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_123__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_123__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When a drainage installation is disconnected from a sewer, the engineer must seal the opening caused by the disconnection and may recover the cost of doing so from the owner of the premises on which the installation is disconnected.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_123__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_123__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a drainage system is connected to or disconnected from the sewer system during a month, charges will be calculated as if the connection or disconnection were made on the first day of the month following the month in which the connection or disconnection took place.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_124" data-eId="sec_124"><h3>124. Technical requirements for drainage installations</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_124__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_124__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All drainage installations shall comply with SANS code 0252 and the Building Regulations.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_125" data-eId="sec_125"><h3>125. Sewer blockages</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may cause or permit an accumulation of grease, oil, fat, solid matter, or any other substance in any trap, tank, or fitting that may cause its blockage or ineffective operation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the owner or occupier of premises has reason to believe that a blockage has occurred in any drainage installation in or on it, he shall take immediate steps to have it cleared.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the owner or occupier of premises has reason to believe that a blockage has occurred in the sewer system, he shall immediately inform the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a blockage occurs in a drainage installation, any work necessary for its removal must be done by, or under the supervision of, a plumber.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should any drainage installation on any premises overflow as a result of an obstruction in the sewer, and if the municipality is reasonably satisfied that the obstruction was caused by objects emanating from the drainage installation, the owner of the premises served by the drainage installation shall be liable for the cost of clearing the blockage.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a blockage has been removed from a drain or portion of a drain which serves two or more premises, the owners are jointly and severally liable for the cost of clearing the blockage.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a blockage in a sanitation system has been removed by the engineer and the removal necessitated the disturbance of an owners paving, lawn or other artificial surface neither the engineer nor the municipality shall be required to restore them to their previous condition and shall not be responsible for any damage to them unless caused by the wrongful act or negligence of the engineer.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_126" data-eId="sec_126"><h3>126. Grease traps</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_126__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_126__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A grease trap of an approved type, size and capacity must be provided in respect of all premises that discharge sewage to on-site sanitation systems or where, in the opinion of the municipality, the discharge of grease, oil and fat is likely to cause an obstruction to the flow in sewers or drains, or to interference with the proper operation of any waste-water treatment plant.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_127" data-eId="sec_127"><h3>127. Industrial grease traps</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_127__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner or manufacturer must ensure that industrial effluent which contains, or which, in the opinion of the municipality is likely to contain, grease, oil, fat of inorganic solid matter in suspension shall, before it is allowed to enter any sewer, is passed through one or more tanks or chambers, of a type, size and capacity designed to intercept and retain such grease, oil, fat or solid matter, that is approved by the engineer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_127__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner or manufacturer must ensure that oil, grease or any other substance which is contained in any industrial effluent or other liquid and which gives off an inflammable or noxious vapour at a temperature of, or exceeding, 20° C must be intercepted and retained in a tank or chamber so as to prevent its entry of into the sewer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_127__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A tank or chamber as referred to in subsection (2) must comply with the following requirements:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">It shall be of adequate capacity, constructed of hard durable materials and water-tight when completed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the water-seal of its discharge pipe shall be not less than 300mm in depth; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">shall be provided with a sufficient number of manhole covers for the adequate and effective removal of grease, oil fat and solid matter.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_127__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any person discharging effluent to a tank or chamber must remove grease, oil, fat or solid matter regularly from the tank or chamber and must maintain a register recording—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the dates on which the tank or chamber was cleaned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the name of any the persons employed by him to clean the tank or chamber or, if he cleaned it himself, that fact that he did so; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_127__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a certificate from the person employed to clean it certifying that the tank or chamber has been cleaned and stating the manner in which the contents of the tank or chamber were disposed of, or, if he cleaned it himself, his own certificate to that effect.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_128" data-eId="sec_128"><h3>128. Mechanical appliances for lifting sewage</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner of any premise must obtain the approval of the engineer before installing any mechanical appliance for the raising or transfer of sewage in terms of the Building Regulations.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Approval must be applied for by a professional engineer and must be accompanied by drawings prepared in accordance with the relevant provisions of the Building Regulations and must show details of the compartment containing the appliance, the sewage storage tank, the stilling chamber and their position, and the position of the drains, ventilation pipes, rising main and the sewer connection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding any approval given in terms of subsection (1), the municipality shall not be liable for any injury, loss or damage to life or property caused by the use, malfunctioning or any other condition arising from the installation or operation of a mechanical appliance for the raising or transfer of sewage unless the injury or damage be caused by the wrongful intentional or negligent act or negligence of an employee of the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every mechanical appliance installed for the raising or transfer of sewage shall be specifically designed for the purpose and shall be fitted with a discharge pipe, sluice valves and non-return valves located in approved positions.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Unless otherwise permitted by the engineer, such mechanical appliances shall be installed in duplicate and each such appliance shall be so controlled that either will immediately begin to function automatically in the event of failure of the other.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every mechanical appliance forming part of a drainage installation shall be located and operated so as to not cause any nuisance through noise or smell or otherwise, and every compartment containing any such appliance must be effectively ventilated.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The maximum discharge rate from any mechanical appliance, and the times between which the discharge may take place, shall be as determined by the engineer who may, at any time, require the owner to install such fittings and regulating devices as may in his opinion, be necessary to ensure that the determined maximum discharge rate shall not be exceeded.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except where sewage storage space is incorporated as an integral part of a mechanical appliance, a sewage storage tank must be provided in conjunction with such appliance.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every sewage storage tank required must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">be constructed of hard, durable materials and must be watertight and the internal surfaces of the walls and floor must be smooth and impermeable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">have a storage capacity below the level of the inlet equal to the quantity of sewage discharged there into it in 24 hours or 900 litres, whichever is the greater quantity; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_9__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">be so designed that the maximum of its sewage content shall be emptied at each discharge cycle of the mechanical appliance.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every storage tank and stilling chamber shall be provided with a ventilation pipe in accordance with the engineer’s specifications.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_9" data-eId="chp_IV__part_9"><h2>Part 9 – Other sanitation services</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_129" data-eId="sec_129"><h3>129. Stables and similar premises</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_129__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_129__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_129__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_129__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may approve the connection of a drainage installation to stables, cowsheds, dairies, kennels, other premises for the accommodation of animals, and tanneries, subject to the payment of all applicable charges and the fulfilment of any condition that the municipality may impose; but approval will be given only if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_129__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_129__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the floor of the premises is paved by impervious materials that are approved by the municipality and graded to a silt trap, grease trap or gully of adequate capacity; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_129__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_129__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">every part of the floor of the premises is covered by a roof, or another protective device, in a way that adequately prevents the entry of rain or storm water into the drainage installation.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_130" data-eId="sec_130"><h3>130. Mechanical food-waste or other disposal units</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The municipality may approve the connection or incorporation of a mechanical waste food, disposal which and any disposal unit or garbage grinder, into a drainage installation that has a capacity in excess of 500W, subject to the payment of all applicable charges and to any condition that the municipality may impose, but approval will be given only if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a water meter is installed by the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the engineer is satisfied that the municipality’s sewerage and sewage treatment system will not be adversely affected; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the installation or incorporation is installed in conformity with the municipality’s by-law relating to electricity.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_10" data-eId="chp_IV__part_10"><h2>Part 10 – Installation work</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_131" data-eId="sec_131"><h3>131. Approval of installation work</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_131__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an owner wishes to have installation work done, he must first obtain the municipality’s written approval.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_131__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Application for the approval referred to in subsection (1) must be made on the prescribed form and shall be accompanied by-</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a charge determined by the municipality, if a charge is determined, and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">copies of all drawings that may be required and approved by the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a certificate by a professional engineer certifying that the installation has been designed in accordance with any applicable SANS Codes.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_131__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Approval given in terms of subsection (1) shall lapse after 24 (twenty-four) months.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_131__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When approval has been given in terms of subsection (1), a complete set of the drawings that have been required and approved by the municipality must be available for inspection at the site at all reasonable times until the work has been completed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_131__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If installation work has been done in contravention of subsections (1) or (2), the municipality may require the owner—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">to rectify the contravention within a specified time;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if work is in progress, to cease the work; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_131__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to remove all work that does not comply with this by-law.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_132" data-eId="sec_132"><h3>132. Persons permitted to do installation and other work</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_132__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person who is not a plumber, or working under the control of a plumber, shall be permitted to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">do installation work other than the replacement or repair of an existing pipe or sanitation fitting;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">inspect, disinfect and test a drainage installation, fire installation or storage tank;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">service, repair or replace a back flow preventer; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">install, maintain or replace a meter provided by an owner in a drainage installation.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_132__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person shall require or engage a person who is not a plumber to do the work referred to in subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_132__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_132__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of subsections (1) and (2), the municipality may permit a person, who is not a plumber, to do installation work at his own premises if they are occupied by himself or his own household, but if permission is given, the work must be inspected and approved by a plumber under the direction of or who has been nominated by, the engineer.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_133" data-eId="sec_133"><h3>133. Testing of drainage installations</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_133__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_133__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No drainage installation, or any part of one, shall be connected to on-site sanitation services nor shall, the municipality’s sanitation system be connected to an existing approved installation, unless any one or more of the following tests have been applied in the presence, and to the satisfaction, of the engineer, before the draining installation has been enclosed:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the interior of every pipe or series of pipes between two points of access shall be inspected throughout its length by means of a mirror and a source of light, and during the inspection, a full circle of light must appear to the observer, and the pipe or series of pipes must be seen to be unobstructed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a smooth ball having a diameter 12mm less than the nominal diameter of the pipe shall, when inserted at the higher end of the pipe, roll down without assistance or interruption to the lower end;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">after all openings to the pipe or series of pipes to be tested, after having been plugged or sealed and after all traps associated with them have been filled with water, air shall be pumped into the pipe or pipes until a manometric pressure of 38mm of water is indicated, after which the pressure must remain greater than 25mm of water for a period of at least 3 (three) minutes without further pumping; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_133__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">all parts of the installation are subjected to and required to withstand an internally applied hydraulic test pressure of not less than a 3m head of water for a period of not less than 10 minutes.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_133__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_133__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the municipality has reason to believe that any drainage installation or any part of it has become defective, it may require the owner of any premises to conduct any or all of the tests prescribed in subsection (1) and, if the installation fails to pass any test, or all the tests, to the satisfaction of the municipality, the municipality may by notice require the owner to take all reasonable measures that may be necessary to enable the installation to satisfy any or all of them.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_134" data-eId="sec_134"><h3>134. Water demand management</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_134__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_134__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of section 32, no flushing urinal that is not user-activated shall be installed or continue to operate in any water installation. All flushing urinals that are not user-activated installed prior to the commencement of these regulations must be converted to user-activated urinals within two years of the commencement of this by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_134__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_134__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No cistern, and related pan designed to operate with such cistern, shall be installed with a cistern capacity of greater than 9 litres and all cisterns not intended for public use shall be fitted with flushing devices allowing interruptible or multiple flushes, provided that such flushing device shall not be required in cisterns with a capacity of 4,5 litres or less.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_11" data-eId="chp_IV__part_11"><h2>Part 11 – General</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_135" data-eId="sec_135"><h3>135. Conflict with other legislation</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_135__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_135__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event of any conflict between any provision of this by-law and National and Provincial legislation, standards, policies or guidelines, the National and Provincial legislation, standards, policies or guidelines shall prevail.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_136" data-eId="sec_136"><h3>136. Revocation of by-laws</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_136__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_136__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of any by-laws previously promulgated by the municipality or by any of the disestablished municipalities now incorporated in the municipality, are hereby repealed as far as they relate to matters provided for in this by-law, and insofar as it has been made applicable to the municipality by the authorisation for the execution of powers and functions in terms of section 84(3) of the Local Government: Municipal Structures Act, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/117" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/117">Act 117 of 1998</a>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_137" data-eId="sec_137"><h3>137. Short title and commencement</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_137__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_137__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This by-law shall be known as the Water Services By-law and commences on the date of publication thereof in the Provincial Gazette.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_IV__part_12" data-eId="chp_IV__part_12"><h2>Part 12 – Quality standards</h2></section></section></span><span class="akn-attachments"><div class="akn-attachment" id="att_1" data-eId="att_1">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule A</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Acceptance of industrial effluent for discharge into the sewage disposal system</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_1/hcontainer_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person shall discharge or cause or permit to be discharged directly or indirectly into any sewer any effluent which—</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">has a temperature exceeding 40 deg. C ;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">has a pH value of less than 6,0 or more than 10,0 at 25 deg. C;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">contains calcium carbide;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any substance which gives off or produces or is liable to give off or produce explosive, inflammable, poisonous or offensive gases or vapours;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any substance which has an open flash point of less than 95 deg. C;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any volatile inflammable solvents or organic solvents immiscible with water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">contains any radio-active waste or isotopes of such nature or in such concentration as do not meet the requirements laid down in the Nuclear Energy Act, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1999/46" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1999/46">Act 46 of 1999</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" of itself or in combination with any other substance—</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">cause a nuisance to the public or any section thereof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">endanger the health of or injure any person, whether employed by the municipality or not;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">have a harmful effect on any sewer or any works or land connected with any sewer or with the conveyance, treatment, purification, disposal or re-use of the effluent, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_x__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">in any way prejudice the disposal or re-use of sewage of effluent after treatment or purification or lead to an effluent which does not meet any requirement laid down in terms of the National Water Act, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/36" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/36">Act 36 of 1998</a>), as amended.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="att_1/hcontainer_2" data-eId="hcontainer_2">RADIO-ACTIVE WASTES</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_1/hcontainer_3" data-eId="hcontainer_3" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Radio-active wastes or isotopes: Such concentration as may be laid down by the Atomic Energy Board or any National Department:</span><span class="akn-p">Provided that, notwithstanding the requirements set out in this Part, the municipality reserves the right to limit the total mass of any substance or impurity discharged per 24 hours into the sanitation system from any premises.</span></span></span><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="att_1/hcontainer_4" data-eId="hcontainer_4">METHOD OF TESTING</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_1/hcontainer_5" data-eId="hcontainer_5" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The method of testing in order to ascertain the concentration of any substance in this Schedule, shall be the test normally used by the municipality for these purposes. Any person discharging any substance referred to in this Schedule shall ascertain the details of the appropriate test from the municipality.</span></span></span></span></span>

</table></span></span><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_2/part_III__subsec_9" data-eId="part_III__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any further information as to kind or character, chemical compositions, concentrations or other properties peculiar to the industrial effluent to be furnished on a separate sheet and attached hereto.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="att_2/part_IV" data-eId="part_IV"><h2>Part IV – Conditions relating to the acceptance of industrial effluent</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/part_IV__para_1" data-eId="part_IV__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant shall attach descriptions and a statement of the dimensions of grease and oil traps, screens, dilution and neutralising tanks and any other provision made for the treatment of the effluent prior to discharge to the sanitation system.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/part_IV__para_2" data-eId="part_IV__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant shall submit to the municipality, if requested, plans showing the reticulation systems on his premises for water and industrial effluent.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/part_IV__para_3" data-eId="part_IV__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant shall, in addition to complying with the provisions of the municipality’s Water Services By-law aimed at the protection of its employees, sewers and treatment plant from damage, comply with any direction concerned with such protection given by the engineer verbally or in writing for the purpose of ensuring the applicant’s compliance with the said by-law.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/part_IV__para_4" data-eId="part_IV__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant shall notify the municipality, as soon as possible after he becomes aware thereof, or at least 14 days before anything is done to cause material alteration in the nature or quantity of the industrial effluent specified in this application or in any of the facts stated by him therein.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/part_IV__para_5" data-eId="part_IV__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant shall, within 30 days from the date of signature of this application, procure an accurately representative sample of not less than 5 litre of the industrial effluent to be discharged into the sewer, which sample shall be free of domestic sewage, and shall submit one half thereof to the municipality for analysis and also submit to the engineer a report on the sample made by an analyst appointed by him: Provided that in the case of a newly established industry the period specified may be extended by the municipality for a period not exceeding six months or such further extended periods as the municipality in its discretion may approve.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/part_IV__para_6" data-eId="part_IV__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant hereby declares and warrants that the information given by him in this form, or otherwise, in connection with this application is, to the best of his knowledge and belief, in all respects correct.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/part_IV__para_7" data-eId="part_IV__para_7"><span class="akn-num">7.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant agrees that the said information, being in all respects correct, shall form the basis on which this application is granted by the municipality.</span><span class="akn-p">Thus done at ..................................... by the applicant this ............... day of ............................20 ............</span><span class="akn-p">...............................................................................</span><span class="akn-p">Signature and capacity of the applicant</span></span></span></section></span></span>
